Major Fire in Henan, Guangzhou 79

More Than Sixty Shops Burned Down

Total Loss Exceeds 700,000 Yuan

Dispatch from Guangzhou: The residential area of Henan is separated from Guangzhou City by a narrow strip of water. Since the completion of the Pearl River Bridge, transportation has become more convenient. In recent years, roads have been opened up one after another in the interior of Henan, and most of the major factories have moved there. However, except for a few main roads, the inner streets of Henan are still very narrow, the air is also turbid, and firefighting is particularly difficult in the event of a fire. Therefore, on the evening of the 24th of this month, an unprecedented major fire broke out in the Yongxing Street area, burning down up to sixty-eight shops, with a loss of no less than 700,000 yuan, which is truly a great disaster. Yongxing Street is located west of Feng'an Bridge in Henan, with shops lining up one after another, backed by a small river. Most of the shops operate in the timber industry. On the evening in question, Hengsheng, No. 104 Yongxing Street, somehow carelessly left a fire in the wood. In an instant, the fire blazed fiercely and was impossible to approach. Before long, it turned into a prairie fire. Fire trucks from various places in Henan and Hebei rushed to put out the fire, and the fire brigade's fireboat also came to the scene to provide assistance. However, Yongxing Street has not yet been opened up into a road, and all the new-style fire trucks could not drive close to the fire scene, only connecting water pipes from a distance to spray water. There were occasional light fire trucks that could get close, but they lacked water and had no great effect. In addition, a southeast wind was blowing that night, and the flames were even more fierce. Fires broke out everywhere near the origin of the fire. Looking from afar, it was like a fire dragon, with flames soaring into the sky. From 10:00 p.m. until about 3:00 a.m. the next morning, the fire was finally extinguished. It is estimated that more than sixty fir wood shops were burned down on Yongxing Street, including Hengsheng, Guang Ping'an, Tong Mao, He Chang, Wen He, Xing Sheng, Ming Ji, Nanhua, Heng Zhan, Yi Cheng, Shun Long, Yuan Ji, Rui Rong, Chang Sheng, Guang Jixiang, Shun Ji, Xiang He, Zhong He, Long Sheng, Cai Chang, and others. Including goods and timber, the total loss was more than 690,000 yuan. Each shop was adjacent to a small canal, and all the timber was stored on the canal bank, blocking more than half of the canal, making it difficult to move. This timber was all burned to ashes. (July 25th)

Hunan Provincial Government Requests Allocation of Cotton and Wheat Loan 80

To Dredge Dongting Lake and Rehabilitate the Jingjiang River

To Promote the Cotton Industry and Maintain Cotton Mills

Dispatch from Changsha: The Hunan Provincial Government believes that the province has suffered from years of military disasters and floods, leading to the bankruptcy of the rural areas. The cotton and rice fields around the lake have also suffered poor harvests due to the backflow of river water and the siltation of Dongting Lake. Although the province has the First Cotton Mill, the cotton produced by the counties around the lake is still not grown and planted widely, resulting in a reduced output. The mill almost entirely purchases foreign cotton. The fundamental solution is to dredge Dongting Lake, rehabilitate the Jingjiang River, and improve the cotton industry, but none of this can be achieved without a large amount of money. In addition, the First Cotton Mill is facing difficulties due to a lack of funds, resulting in a summer shutdown. It will be difficult to resume operations without special fundraising relief. Recently, the central government's cotton and wheat loan has been successfully secured. A request has been submitted to the Executive Yuan to allocate the loan in order to proceed in various ways and benefit the people. The memorandum states: "It is our understanding that our country's production is backward, coupled with years of military disasters and floods, the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy. The predicament is particularly severe in Hunan Province. Hunan has always been known as an agricultural province, and the ability of the people of Hunan to have sufficient food and clothing depends entirely on the abundant harvests of cotton and rice from the fields around the lake. However, since Dongting Lake has been subject to silting from four inlets, disasters have occurred repeatedly, and harvests have been poor for nine out of ten years. Taking cotton alone, due to the failure to improve seeds, the failure to promote cultivation, and the losses from floods, the quality of the output is poor and the output is reduced, making it difficult to supply the needs of the province's cotton mills. As a result, the cotton mills purchase all foreign cotton as raw materials, which increases the cost and makes it impossible to compete with foreign yarn. Business is stagnant, and there is a risk that it cannot be sustained. In order to rescue the rural areas and revitalize industry and commerce, nothing can be achieved without a large amount of money to develop water conservancy and improve and promote the cotton industry. Fortunately, the central government's cotton and wheat loan has been successfully secured. The Yuan's department must determine the principles for allocating this loan, and a large part of this loan will be used as funding for cotton production. We hereby request that the loan be allocated to develop water conservancy and the cotton industry and to maintain the cotton mills, as follows: ㈠ It is our understanding that since the Baichichi inlet of Dongting Lake has been subject to backflow of river water, the bottom of the lake has gradually silted up and the surface of the lake has become increasingly narrow. In recent years, sandbars have been densely distributed, and the dikes are adjacent to each other. Reeds are everywhere, and the original shape of Dongting Lake is no longer recognizable. The old course of the Jingjiang River (the section of the Yangtze River from Jingzhou to Chenglingji, commonly known as the Jingjiang River) has been reduced in flow by more than half due to the diversion of river water into the lake, and the flow rate has also decreased accordingly. Sand and mud have settled, not only raising the bottom of the river, but also increasing the islands in the middle of the river at the same time. The silting situation is exactly the same as that of Dongting Lake. Looking at the downstream, since the Chongming section of Hankou City, the Yangtze River basin has been surrounded by Dongting Lake for hundreds of miles due to the river water entering the lake, losing its high-level momentum and reducing its power to wash sand into the sea, resulting in the stagnation of silt and the formation of islands. Such as Hankou Beach, Sanjiangkou, Daijia Island, Zhangjia Island, Yaojia Island, Taizi Islet, Chongwen Island, Desheng Island, Liang Island, and Huguang Island, all of which lie across the heart of the river, blocking the water flow. Therefore, in recent decades, the Yangtze River basin has suffered floods every time, and the provinces along the river, from Hunan to Jiangsu, have not been spared. In 1931, the rich areas along the river were reduced to swamps, which is clear proof. Tracing the origin of the disaster, the floods are actually due to the siltation of the Yangtze River, the disrepair of Dongting Lake, and the unrehabilitated old course of the Jingjiang River. Therefore, if we want to eliminate floods, we must first dredge the Yangtze River, and dredging the river must start with dredging Dongting Lake and the Jingjiang River. According to the research results of water conservancy experts, the plan for dredging Dongting Lake and the Jingjiang River is nothing more than three points: ㈠ Dredge the Jingjiang River to straighten the bends and smooth the flow. ㈡ Excavate the Yue Li Canal to divert water into the river, and build gates downstream of the four inlets of Ouchi, Taiping, Songzi, and Tiaoxian to regulate the Jingjiang River water and prevent Dongting Lake from being silted up again. ㈢ Widen the outlet of Dongting Lake, excavate Linxiang Ma'anshan, and remove Xiyang Island in the river to allow the river water to flow smoothly and prevent it from overflowing and causing disasters. The above three points are actually the preliminary work to dredge the Yangtze River, which is beneficial to the national economy and the people's livelihood. However, due to the exhaustion of local financial resources, it has not been possible to carry out the work. In addition, our Hunan is located in a remote area, the waterways are divergent, and the harm of Dongting Lake silting up and the situation in the Yangtze River basin are not well known by the central government. We will briefly describe the outline and pray for inspection and verification. For the sake of relief, please allocate the cotton and wheat loan to dredge Dongting Lake and the Jingjiang River to avoid floods and benefit the people. This is the first request to allocate the loan to develop water conservancy. ㈡

It is our understanding that our country is founded on agriculture, but the import of agricultural products has been increasing year by year. Among them, the import of cotton goods is very large, accounting for two-fifths to one-third of the value of imported goods. The shortage of raw cotton prevents the development of the spinning industry, and the import of cotton goods is increasing, which in turn leads to a decline in people's livelihood. It is urgent to find a way to rescue the situation. For the sake of improving and promoting the cotton industry in Hunan Province, the Cotton Industry Experimental Farm was established in 1930 to study and improve varieties and methods. A branch farm was established in Changde, and breeding farms were established in Huarong, Lixian, and Hengyang. Significant results have been achieved in the domestication of American cotton and the improvement of Chinese cotton. Later, the cooperation method was used to promote it in rural areas. Personnel were dispatched to guide borrowing and planting technology to alleviate economic difficulties. In less than two years, cooperation has reached 500,000 mu. The output and quality of the products are indeed higher than that of local cotton. However, at a time when the national rural economy is declining, the task of revitalization cannot be fully rescued by the efforts of one province or one city. The central government should take the lead in planning and allocating large amounts of money to carry out the promotion on a large scale, so that the effectiveness will be greater. It is our understanding that 3.28 million US dollars should be allocated from this American cotton loan as funding for cotton industry improvement and promotion, and the cotton areas in the two lakes of China that already have a foundation should be started to promote the cotton industry and stop the leakage. This is the second request to allocate the loan to develop the cotton industry. ㈢ It is our understanding that cotton is the raw material for cotton yarn. If cotton is abundant, the cost of cotton yarn is low. If cotton is scarce, the cost of cotton yarn is high. Last year, due to the poor harvest of cotton in various provinces, the price of cotton was expensive. Also, because the rural economy was sluggish, the price of cotton yarn was low. Cotton and cotton yarn went in opposite directions. Cotton mills across the country suffered heavy losses and fell into an unsustainable state. The Hunan First Cotton Mill is the only state-run cotton mill in Hunan Province, and it is also the only factory that complies with the factory law. However, due to the lack of funds, it is facing difficulties, which is especially true compared to other factories in the country. Therefore, the summer shutdown was unavoidable, waiting for the new cotton to be on the market before resuming operations. If the new cotton crop fails again and prices remain high, the factory will have to shut down for a long period of time. It is proposed to approve the monthly allocation of 5,000 dan of American cotton within the American cotton allocation, and also request that 10,000 dan of 7/8 inch middling cotton be allocated in advance when the first batch of American cotton arrives in Shanghai, so as to start operations as soon as possible. As for how the price will be determined, it will be handled in accordance with the unified regulations. This is the third request to allocate American cotton to maintain cotton mills. The above three items are all essential plans for Hunan Province. In addition to sending Yuan Hui, the director of the Hunan Cotton Industry Experimental Farm, to Beijing to present the case in person, we have prepared a memorandum and presented it to your Yuan for examination. We beseech you to consider the difficulties in Hunan and approve the request to allocate the loan and American cotton to develop water conservancy and the cotton industry and maintain the cotton mills, and await your instructions. (July 21st)

Jiang Song

Secretary of the Supervisory Yuan, Huang Renzhong, Visited Songjiang Again Yesterday 81

The previous report stated that Huang Renzhong, Secretary of the Supervisory Yuan, accompanied Supervisory Committee Member Gao Yihan to Songjiang to inspect the state of official governance, public security, and education. Now it is learned that a gentleman from Songjiang had previously submitted a petition to the Supervisory Yuan accusing the liquidation committee of fraud after the collapse of the Songjiang Bank, amounting to tens of thousands of yuan. The Supervisory Yuan believed that the matter concerned the public and private finances of Songjiang and was of great importance, so it dispatched Huang to investigate. It is now learned that Huang visited the Songjiang County Court and the liquidation office again yesterday (the 1st) at 8:00 a.m. to review the entire file, accompanied by President Wang and Chief Prosecutor Zhu, to inspect the prison and detention center, and then went to other institutions to inquire about the case. It is said that many suspicious points have been discovered.

Suzhou

Opposition to Cars Driving in the City 82

Citizens Zhang Shoupeng and others previously submitted a petition to the county government requesting permission for cars to drive in the city for the convenience of the people. The county government has forwarded it to the Department of Civil Affairs for review. Yesterday (the 1st), Xu Liangsheng and others directly submitted a petition to the Department of Civil Affairs, stating that the Jinmen South New Bridge has not yet been rebuilt, the streets in the city have not yet been widened in general, and the passage of cars is of no benefit to the common people, expressing their opposition.

The Entire Town of Majiaqiao Robbed 83

Fengjiaqiao Town, located thirty li away from Jiaxing City, has a total of more than one hundred shops. At about 10:00 p.m. on the night of July 30, more than twenty lake bandits suddenly arrived, all armed with guns. They first surrounded the town's defense team and confiscated five rifles, and then searched and robbed each household one by one. It took an hour for them to finish. It is estimated that the most heavily robbed were a pawnshop and two foreign goods and cloth shops. The bandits fled with their loot towards Jiangsu. Yesterday (the 1st), the Third District of the Jiangsu Water Police received a report that these lake bandits were a combination of three gangs from Henan, Anhui, and Jiangbei. The bandit leader's name is Tang Jinbiao. They are currently entering Jiangsu Province from Taihu Lake, so they immediately ordered the team to pay attention to blocking and suppressing them.

Another Fugitive in the Feiyun Steamer Robbery Arrested 84

After the execution of the bandit leader Shi Jiaxing in the Feiyun steamer robbery case in Dongshan, in which Ms. Fu Zhongde, the principal of Zhongxiu Elementary School, was killed, the fugitive bandit Hua Fusheng and others in the case were wanted by the official authorities with a reward. Now it has been learned that Mao Wenlong, a detective from the Third District of the Water Police, together with Pei Xuan, the captain of the Seventh Team, captured Liu Fusheng in Wuzhen, Zhejiang Province, the day before yesterday (the 31st). Yesterday (the 1st), he was escorted to the Third District of the Suzhou Water Police for investigation. Liu is 18 years old, nicknamed Xiaoguangdan, and is the adopted son of the executed bandit leader Shi Jiaxing. Before his arrest, he was a soldier in the anti-smuggling camp in Wuzhen.

Wuxi

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes a Large Quantity of Enemy Goods 85

The local Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association received a secret report the day before yesterday evening stating that Nanhuo shops such as Lida, Taizao along the river outside the North Gate, and Yongmao at the Jieganting Lane entrance entrusted the Taichang steamer to secretly transport a large quantity of enemy goods, kelp, to Wuxi for sale, and stored the goods in the public ice factory in order to avoid attention. The chairman of the association, Wei Zhiwen, issued an inspection warrant and dispatched inspectors to inspect. As a result, 70 pieces of enemy goods, kelp, were seized and sealed up immediately. A report was made to the Anti-Japanese Association to await identification and punishment.

Three Women Commit Suicide 86

Xu Deyong, a migrant from another province who opened a tiger stove in Houqi Street outside the North Gate of this county, married Zhang, who was thirty-two years old. The couple had a good relationship. Recently, Zhang suffered from abdominal pain due to eating melon during her menstrual period. Although she sought medical treatment, it was still ineffective, and she had spent a lot of money, accumulating debts. Zhang felt both physically and mentally distressed, so she hanged herself at about 4:00 a.m. yesterday. Also, a woman surnamed Mou at the bottom of Jiangyin Lane was gambling in Zhang the carpenter's shop nearby the day before yesterday and was discovered and fined by the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. After returning home, she was reprimanded by her husband. In a moment of anger, she hanged herself. When her husband discovered her, he sent her to the hospital for treatment, but she died. Also, Hu, the wife of Ji Xixiang, a resident of No. 47 Taiping Lane outside Guangfu Gate, also committed suicide out of anger after being detained for gambling. Doctors Xu Shilin and Wang Shiqi were asked to treat her, but she died.

Kidnapping Suspect Arrested and Sent to Beijing 87

A traveler from Yixing came to the Qitai Inn on Tongyun Road a dozen days ago, accompanied by a fashionable young woman. He claimed to be named Wang Changsheng and behaved extravagantly. Visitors came in an endless stream. Then, someone secretly reported to the headquarters of the Fifth Regiment of the Wuxi Garrison that the man was impersonating a military police inspector and engaging in deception in Wuxi. The regiment headquarters dispatched troops to detain the man and woman. According to his confession, his name was Lin Guoguang, a native of Zhenjiang, and her name was Ling Shunchuan. They came to Wuxi from Suzhou this time. Three years ago, he committed a kidnapping case involving a certain family in Yixing, extorting a large sum of money, and impersonating an inspector. Subsequently, the Yixing County Government issued an arrest warrant. According to the regiment headquarters' confession, the woman was found to be unrelated and was released on bail. Lin was escorted to the Nanjing Military Police Headquarters for interrogation yesterday.

Serious Locust Plague in the Twelfth District of Changzhou 88

Due to prolonged drought in the Dong'an Town area of the Twelfth District of Wu County, most of the rice seedlings have withered. Unexpectedly, a large number of flying locusts have recently been discovered. At first, they ate reeds, and then they nibbled on the shore. It is estimated that four or five hills of lakeside rice fields have been eaten. Farmers are panicked and their situation is deplorable. The town chief, Jiang Guoyou, has reported to the county government for instructions and has also united with various villages to organize a locust-catching team to engage in extermination. After receiving the report, the county government put it forward for discussion at the county government meeting on the 31st and decided to order the relevant local authorities to supervise the villagers to jointly exterminate the locusts and send personnel to investigate.

The Jiangyin Party Committee Case Expands 89

Chen Xiping, a standing committee member of the Executive Committee of the County Party Headquarters, was accused of dereliction of duty and bribery by Yao Mingzhi and others. The Party Headquarters also reported the case of Dong Bingying, the chief of general affairs, for falsely accusing the documentation. The Jiangsu High Court designated the Wuxi Court to hear the case. Although Zhang Jianmen and others mediated repeatedly without success, yesterday (the 31st) was the second court session. Chen Xiping and others arrived in court in accordance with the summons, but Huang Bingying suddenly went to the County Party Headquarters office at about 8:00 p.m. on the 30th and forcibly took away the oath frame of the executive supervisory committee members and the case files, claiming to be the power of a candidate member. Shen Qinru and other Party Headquarters staff members tried to stop him without success. On the 31st, the Party Headquarters sent a letter to the county to arrest Huang. After interrogation, the police were ordered to guard him. The oath was presented by Yao Mingzhi to the Wuxi Court for verification of the seals. At 10:00 a.m., Prosecutor Zhou interrogated them. Because Huang Bingying and Zhou Linyun did not arrive, the interrogation was postponed. Currently, the case is getting bigger and it is difficult to resolve it for the time being.

Nantong Thoroughly Investigates Embankment Collapse Corruption 90

Nantong's southwest is adjacent to the river and the collapse is very serious. In the past, the late gentleman Zhang Jian raised more than one million yuan to build eighteen stone embankments to compete with the water for land, with good results. After Zhang's death, the embankment maintenance association was taken over by the Construction Bureau, changing it from a people-run to a government-run organization. Over the years, the embankment maintenance fees collected from the field tax have been extremely large, but the money has been exhausted. The old embankments have not been repaired and have gradually collapsed. Currently, Langshan is about to enter the river, and the county people are in an uproar. Recently, the embankment maintenance association's false reporting of wages and construction costs was revealed. The chairman, Li Zhenru, has secretly left Nantong. Currently, county gentlemen Chen Chen and others have asked the county government to thoroughly investigate the matter in order to dispel public doubts.

Hangzhou Police Cause Death During Gambling Arrest 91

Zhu Changfa, a resident of No. 9 Zhongzheng Lane, Dongjie Road, Hangzhou, was fifty-four years old and worked as a silk weaver. He had two sons and one daughter, all of whom were grown up. The night before last (the 31st) at 2:00 a.m., he was gambling at the management of Wang Yangshi, the of the Economic Society, at the Baoshu Pagoda on Baoshi Mountain in the West Lake. The police in charge learned of this and dispatched Police Chief Wang Yaochen to lead police to arrest them. Before reaching the location, the gamblers heard the news and scattered and fled. However, Zhu Changfa, due to his old age and the late hour, could not distinguish the path. He ran out of the back door and fell down the mountain. His companions hired a car to take him home, but he died halfway due to his injuries. The head of the gambling house, Wang Yangshi, was summoned to the Eighth Precinct of the First Division and sent to the bureau for interrogation.

Local News

The National Salvation Donation Investigation Committee is Established

Publicly Electing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Trade Unions, etc. as Standing Committee Members

Deliberating on Investigation Methods and Submitting Them to the Authorities for Record

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Trade Unions, Lawyers Association, Accountants Association, and other groups, believing that the total amount of donations from all walks of life across the country to comfort General Ma Zhanshan reached approximately 20 million yuan, while Ma himself claimed to have only received more than 1.71 million yuan, convened a meeting of various groups at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m. in order to clarify the truth. The Shanghai Municipal National Salvation Donation Investigation Committee was established, and investigation methods were discussed. The details are recorded on the left:

Participating Organizations 92

The attendees of yesterday's meeting included representatives from the following organizations: Luo Qinghua of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Wang Weizhen and Shen Junru of the Lawyers' Association, He Yuanming and Wang Haifan of the Accountants' Association, Zhu Xuefan and Long Peiyun of the General Labor Union, Lu Jingshi and Huang Gongfu of the National Postal Workers' General Union, Hu Fengxiang, Zhu Yangwu, and Zhang Dafu of the First Special District Municipal Federation, Huang Xianggu and Mao Yun of the Second Special District Municipal Federation, Tao Baichuan and Wu Xiu of the Municipal Education Association, Yu Zhenhui and Zhang Huijun of the Municipal Farmers' Association, Liu Xuru and Xue Guangqian of the United Association of Universities, Wu Zhenjin and Shen Zuru of the Secondary Education United Association, Gao Zongjing, Sun Deming, and Shen Shiying of the Middle School United Association, and over thirty other individuals. Lu Jingshi was elected as chairman, and Zhu Yangwu as secretary.

Chairman's Report 93

Following the formalities, the chairman delivered a report, stating in brief: "Since the September 18th Incident, our nation's populace, driven by patriotic fervor, has risen up in response, enthusiastically donating funds to aid the soldiers fighting against Japan and fulfilling their national duty. However, after General Ma Zhanshan's arrival in Shanghai, the amount of anti-Japanese donations he declared received does not match the widely reported figures, causing widespread doubt. If this is not thoroughly investigated, it will severely impact the future of patriotic donations. Therefore, to clarify the truth, we have convened representatives from various organizations to discuss methods of investigation in order to dispel public suspicion. We hope that all representatives will express their opinions to facilitate the process."

Resolutions Passed 94

(A) Regarding whether to formally establish an organization, it was resolved that: (I) An organization should be formally established, with organizations as the unit; (II) All organizations attending today's meeting will be members of the committee; (III) The Great Education Association and the Municipal Fishermen's Association will be invited to join; (IV) The organization will be named the "Shanghai Municipal All Circles Investigation Committee for National Salvation Donations"; (V) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce will serve as the office address; (VI) The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, and the Municipal Education Association will be elected as standing committee members; (VII) The secretariat will be designated by the standing committee members; (VIII) The next meeting will be held next Friday at 2:00 PM, convened by the General Labor Union. (B) Regarding expenses, each organization will share the cost equally. The standing committee will draft a budget to be submitted for discussion. (C) Regarding the investigation method, it was resolved that: (I) All anti-Japanese military generals should be notified to report the accounts of donations received to the committee; (II) All donation organizations should be instructed to submit their donation accounts for review by the committee within one week of receiving the notice; (III) Opinions on investigating donations will be solicited from all sectors. (D) Regarding the committee's application for record filing with Party and government authorities, it was resolved to pass the motion. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Standing Committee Meeting 95

Following the adjournment of the meeting, the Standing Committee Meeting was immediately convened. Representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, the Lawyers' Association, the Accountants' Association, and the Municipal Education Association, including Luo Qinghua and Zhu Xuefan, were in attendance. Luo Qinghua chaired the meeting, and after the report, discussions began. (I) Regarding the proposal to designate daily routine duties and rotate office work, it was resolved that: Mondays - Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Tuesdays - General Labor Union, Wednesdays - Lawyers' Association, Thursdays - Accountants' Association, Fridays - Municipal Education Association, Saturdays and Sundays - Office closed. (II) Regarding the Standing Committee meeting dates, it was resolved that meetings would be held every Tuesday and Friday at 2:00 PM. (III) Regarding the proposal to designate the Municipal Chamber of Commerce as the General Affairs Department to handle documents, general affairs, accounting, and other matters, it was resolved to pass the motion. (IV) Regarding drafting the budget for the committee's expenses, it was resolved that the General Affairs Department would draft a budget immediately. (V) Regarding the immediate implementation of resolutions decided at the joint meeting, it was resolved that the General Affairs Department and others would comply.

Totaling over 46,000 Yuan in Foreign Currency

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday announced the amount of condolence donations remitted to General Ma Zhanshan as follows: (I) Direct Remittance by the Chamber: Taken directly from collected donations and remitted; On November 14th, 20th year of the Republic, 10,000 yuan in foreign currency was telegraphed to Heilongjiang via the Bank of China; On November 25th of the same year, 25,000 yuan in foreign currency was telegraphed to Harbin; On December 22nd, 8,790 yuan and 7 jiao 2 fen in foreign currency was telegraphed to Harbin. These three remittances were published in various newspapers on December 21st, 20th year of the Republic. Ma Zhanshan Publicly Announces Detailed Amount of Donations Received 97

Totaling over 1,713,000 Yuan

Names of Donors Lost in the Black Province

The total amount of condolence donations from all sectors of the country to Ma Zhanshan reached 20 million yuan, but Ma himself claimed to have received only over 1.7 million yuan. The difference between the two figures amounts to more than 18 million yuan. Therefore, all parties requested that Ma publicly announce the donations he received and thoroughly investigate the exact amount of the donations and the procedures of the handlers to prevent embezzlement by a few. Yesterday, Ma Zhanshan provided a detailed explanation of the donations received from the start of the resistance in November of the 20th year of the Republic until his retreat back to the country, along with a list of relief items. We have specially transcribed them together as follows:

Ma's Statement on Receipts 98

General Ma Zhanshan yesterday issued a letter regarding the receipts and procedures. Respectfully, I, Zhanshan, fought against the Japanese and their puppets in Heilongjiang for a year. As Heilongjiang is a border province with limited resources, and during times of turmoil, financial resources were cut off, and military expenses could not be met. If it were not for the generous donations from compatriots at home and abroad, which boosted the morale of the troops and provided sustenance, it would have been impossible to sustain the fight for so long. I am deeply grateful for their enthusiasm. Now, I will describe the method of receiving donations and the circumstances before and after. The methods of remittance were divided into two categories: banks and post offices. The banks were further divided into Chinese and foreign banks. The locations where Zhanshan received donations were in Heilongjiang Province before November 24th, 20th year of the Republic, and in Hailun and Harbin from November 25th, 20th year of the Republic to February 2nd, 21st year of the Republic, divided into three locations. Except for the 85,000 yuan remitted by the Shanghai Bank of China to the Heilongjiang Branch of the Bank of China on November 13th and 14th of the 20th year of the Republic, which was immediately acknowledged by telegram, all remittances directly sent to Zhanshan by post office were returned with the name stamp affixed to the remittance receipt, and letters and telegrams of thanks were sent immediately. For remittances sent to Harbin by bank, a special commissioner was sent to Harbin to handle the receipt procedures with the bank, with a printed triplicate form prepared for filling out (but before the triplicate form was prepared, 22 receipts with Zhanshan's name stamp in ink were used). The procedure was that the bank provided a detailed list of the name of the remitter for each remittance, stating the address and amount. The commissioner filled out the triplicate form accordingly. Each form was affixed with the four-character "Ma Zhanshan Seal" on the amount of the remittance, below the recipient's name, and where the stamp was affixed. One copy was given to the bank, one copy was sent by the bank to the remitter, and one copy was kept for filing. After the commissioner completed the procedures, he recorded the amount received on a given day in a book for verification and then sent the filed copy along with the remitter's name list to Hailun. The personnel in charge of receiving condolence donations at the慰劳招待处established in Hailun made detailed registrations and were responsible for safekeeping and filing. Zhanshan then sent letters and telegrams of thanks separately. According to statistics, the amount received in Heilongjiang up to February 22nd, 21st year of the Republic, converted into various currencies, was approximately 1,380,710 yuan, 0 jiao, and 3 fen. On April 2nd, 21st year of the Republic, Zhanshan swiftly left the province for Heihe, and all documents could not be carried. Therefore, the detailed records and files were left in the provincial capital. Fortunately, a book kept by the personnel sent to Harbin was still kept by the personnel. However, this book was originally only used to verify the amount received on a given day and did not clearly record who remitted from where. This is the reason why the names of remitters or organizations cannot be listed in detail in this disclosure of the received funds. I, Zhanshan, think that since Zhanshan departed from Heihe, his whereabouts have been uncertain. There was no designated bank or fixed location for receiving remittances from various places. If any donors have not received the above-mentioned triplicate form, the receipt with Zhanshan's name stamp, and the letter or telegram of thanks, I am afraid there may be errors. However, banks and post offices all have prescribed procedures, and it should not be difficult to clarify the truth through investigation. As for the funds handled by the Heihe Provincial Government, Ma Kui, Duan Zhongfan, Deng Wenshao, Binshan, and Li Zhongyi in Pinghu, and the funds received by Zhanshan in Shanghai after returning to the country, the names and locations of the remitters will be disclosed in detail. In short, for the funds received, please ask the remitting institutions to investigate the original circumstances. Zhanshan, relying on your high regard, should also express his gratitude. All the funds disposed of are listed in the list for your perusal. In addition, the funds received by the Liaojihei Support Association have considerable procedures. The condolence items from all sectors in Harbin and other places were either carried to the front line with the funds for distribution to the troops or directly distributed by the donors. Because the files are in the province and have not been brought out, the names and quantities of all donors, organizations, and items have not been listed one by one. I hereby declare this.

Ministry of Finance Rectifies Subsidiary Currency 100

Coordinating and Strictly Prohibiting Private Minting

First Establish Measures to Ban Transportation

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, formerly to ban inferior corner measures, intends to request the central government to concentrate coinage rights, strictly prohibit private minting, and adjust the number of positive auxiliary coins from time to time, so as to average, should immediately present the municipal government, transferred to the Ministry of Finance for approval, The Ministry of Finance is now coordinating measures for the rectification of auxiliary currency, the illegal inferior corners on the market should be strictly prohibited from private minting, so we will first formulate measures to ban the transportation of silver corners, and then coordinate and strictly prohibit private minting, The current ban on the circulation of silver corners is recorded below, (I) All those who transport inferior light corners of private minting, hoping to exercise profit, when the checkpoints are found, should be handled in accordance with these measures, (II) Before the implementation of the new coinage method, all single silver corners with a total weight of 7 minutes 2 li of Kuping, containing 5 minutes 04 hao of pure silver, are temporarily allowed to circulate according to local customs, (III) Whether single-quality silver corners, if they do not meet the weight and fineness of the preceding item, they are inferior light corners, (IV) All inferior light corners that are found should be melted into silver in their entirety, the proceeds of the silver, after removing the cost of handling and melting, should be deducted 20% for public use, and then from the public fund, 20% should be given as a reward, the remaining silver should be returned to the original transporter for collection, (V) All non-inferior light corners, regardless of single or double corners, the number is within 500 coins, allowing merchants to freely transport, by the customs inspection and release, if more than 500 coins, should apply to the customs supervision office of the place of departure for a passport, before loading, (VI) When the customs supervision office issues a passport, it should first ascertain the declared number, type, and location of transportation, and fill it in the passport, (VII) The customs found that the transportation of silver corners without a license, or the transportation of silver corners more than the passport, except for the inferior light corners, should be handled in accordance with the above melting and sharing method, if it is a non-inferior light coin, 3% should be given as a reward, and the remainder should be returned,

After the Signing of the North China Truce Agreement

Dumping of Japanese Goods in China 112

Last Month Suddenly Exceeded 50 Million Yuan. The World Sales Market for Japanese Goods, After Encountering Serious Setbacks, Actively Sought to Make China Its Outlet for Dumping. According to Industry Sources, Since the Signing of the North China Truce Agreement, the Japanese Have Been Actively Recovering and Developing Sales Markets in South and North China, with Significant Progress. The General Situation Is Recorded Below.

Alarming Numbers 113

Before the signing of the North China Truce Agreement, the total value of Japanese goods imported each month was about 20 to 30 million yuan. After the end of the military conflict, Japanese merchants, under the urgent orders of the government, mobilized simultaneously in the north and south to resume business. Last month, it suddenly exceeded 50 million yuan, with sales in North China accounting for 30 million yuan and South China accounting for 20 million yuan. Especially in North China, in addition to using their own diplomatic means, the Japanese also used Chinese political forces to prevent and reject Japanese goods. As a result, the anti-Japanese movement in North China disappeared, and the Japanese were able to make further progress and gain a monopoly on the commercial market. Any British and American goods, whether industrial products, pharmaceuticals, daily necessities, or electrical appliances, that sold well in North China, the Japanese would use dumping tactics to prevent their development. For example, in the case of light bulbs, most of the light bulbs used in North China were domestic products, and well-known light bulbs produced by British and German merchants. Recently, most of them have been Japanese goods. Cases of counterfeiting are endless. The punished are Chinese, but in fact, the Chinese are only working for the benefit of the enemy and are not Chinese products.

Evasion of Customs Duties 114

In order to help Chinese industry and commerce defeat European and American industry and commerce, the Japanese use dumping as the only means. However, many goods are limited by cost and cannot be reduced. Therefore, in the Fujian and Guangdong areas, they use complex foreign merchant relationships to collude with Chinese people and organize large-scale tax evasion agencies to reduce tariffs and lower costs. Customs is unable to prevent it.

Promotion Methods 115

In order to broaden sales channels, the Japanese use both lending and cheap prices to entice Chinese merchants and traitors to set up sales agencies, hanging up Chinese store signs. There are more than a dozen such stores in Shanghai. There are several or dozens of such stores in Hankou, Jiujiang, Qingdao, Jinan, Fuzhou, Guangzhou, and other places. The method is very convenient. For example, if you purchase 100 yuan of Japanese goods from such a store, you will be charged an additional 5 yuan for insurance. The store is responsible for transporting the goods to the destination. If the goods are seized by the Anti-Japanese Association on the way or at the destination, the store will acknowledge the loss and compensate the full amount. Even if it amounts to tens of thousands or hundreds of thousands of yuan, there will be no objection. The provision of fire and water insurance is especially credible. Most cold-blooded merchants flock to it, and Japanese goods are sold smoothly.

Forming Large Companies 116

Because Japanese goods have been severely rejected in the British, Indian, and Dutch territories, resulting in significant setbacks, the Japanese manufacturers have urged the government to order Mitsubishi and Mitsui, which are deeply rooted in China, to actively resume import and export trade. This has now become a reality. Furthermore, they plan to set up four large companies in Shanghai, similar in scale to Sincere, Wing On, and Lane Crawford established by the British. They also plan to set up dozens of small-scale department stores, using low prices as a selling point, attempting to monopolize commercial power. This is gradually taking shape, and it is expected that they will all open this year, adding retail aggression to wholesale aggression.

Active Japanese Ships 117

There are a total of 21 Japanese ships operating on our inland rivers, on six routes: Shanghai-Hankou, Shanghai-Yichang, Hankou-Yichang, Hankou-Changsha, Hankou-Xiangtan, and Yichang-Chongqing. They are all owned by Nissin Kisen Kaisha, with ship names such as Luoyang, Fengyang, Nanyang, Xiangyang, Ruiyang, Dafu, Dali, Dazhen, Daji, Yueyang, Xinyang, Dangyang, Yiyang, Changyang, Chongyang, Daheng, Xiangjiang, Yuanjiang, Wuling, Fuling, and Jialing. After the Shanghai Incident, followed by the war in North China, due to the strong resistance from the Chinese people, except for a few that did not stop to maintain routes, the rest were irregular voyages. Now, they plan to take advantage of the opportunity to gradually recover. In addition to obtaining exclusive transportation rights for Japanese goods on the Yangtze River, they are also secretly recruiting brokers in Shanghai and Hankou to lobby merchants, using the slogan of reducing freight rates. Water and fire insurance are included in the package. Once this campaign is mature, all the ships will be fully restored. It is expected that the shipping industry will undergo drastic changes at that time. If the Chinese people do not quickly sever ties with Japanese goods and Japanese ships, then Chinese money will turn into Japanese guns and cannons to destroy our cities and slaughter our compatriots, and will not stop until we are all killed and exterminated. The Executive Yuan Decides on Measures for Foreigners to Lease Land 119

Strictly Enforce the Provisional Regulations on the Lease of Land and Property

Local Authorities Should Properly Handle Unauthorized Transfers

The Municipal Land Bureau yesterday received an instruction from the Municipal Government, which was forwarded from the Executive Yuan, ordering strict enforcement of the Provisional Regulations on the Lease of Land and Houses by Foreign Churches in the Interior. If Chinese people violate the regulations and transfer land to foreign churches or foreign people without authorization, the local government should handle it carefully and notify the Ministries of Interior and Foreign Affairs for record and verification. The Executive Yuan's circular and the results of the review are recorded separately below.

Order from the Executive Yuan 120

The Executive Yuan's circular states: "Previously, a letter was received from the Central News Agency Committee, forwarded by the Standing Committee from the Hunan Provincial Executive Committee, stating that it was found that residents in the interior were selling national land to foreign nationals or foreign religious followers, and the government should impose sanctions. Also, if foreigners lease land from residents in the interior, should it be submitted to the local government for approval, and what are the procedures, and are there any relevant legal regulations? The committee did not dare to speculate on the above two points and therefore forwarded the document to request instructions. The Executive Yuan was ordered to investigate and reply. In response, the Ministries of Interior, Foreign Affairs, and Judicial Administration were jointly asked to review and verify the matter. They all stated that foreigners in the interior, except for churches that can use the name of the church to lease land in accordance with the Provisional Regulations on the Lease of Houses by Foreign Churches in the Interior, have no right to lease land. As for residents in the interior who sell national land to foreign nationals or foreign religious followers, in addition to revoking the transfer, the land sellers should be given administrative punishment. However, there are no such regulations in the current laws. Whether punishment should be given and how it should be given should be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. The above was submitted to the 133rd meeting of the Executive Yuan and resolved to be replied to by the Ministries of Interior and Foreign Affairs. Now, the results of the joint review and verification have been reported. The report was submitted to the 116th meeting of the Executive Yuan, amended, and passed. In addition to sending a letter to the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee for investigation and forwarding to the subordinate local governments, all should comply with the handling."

Review Results 121

Chinese people in the interior who transfer land to foreign people or violate the Provisional Regulations on the Lease of Land and Houses by Foreign Churches in the Interior and transfer land to foreign churches should, in principle, be sanctioned. However, there are no regulations in the current laws. It seems that a legislative procedure should be followed to formulate legal regulations for the sanctions. However, this plan must take into account all aspects of the situation and cannot be formulated in a short period of time. Before these regulations are formulated, the Executive Yuan should strictly order the provincial and municipal governments to instruct the local governments to strictly enforce the Provisional Regulations on the Lease of Land and Houses by Foreign Churches in the Interior. If Chinese people violate these regulations or treaties and transfer land to foreign churches or foreign people without authorization, the local government should carefully handle the matter, taking into account the circumstances, and notify the Ministries of Interior and Foreign Affairs for record and verification.

Recommendations from the Industrial Safety Association

Safety and Health Facilities for the Rubber Industry 123

The Special Committee Approved the Draft Recommendation Yesterday

Clarifying the Causes of Fire and Principles of Fire Prevention

A Total of Twelve Items of Necessary Facilities

After rubber factories such as the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory were successively ordered to suspend work or relocate by the concession authorities due to lack of safety equipment, the Industrial Safety Association, jointly formed by various factories, specially organized a Special Committee for the Rubber Industry to study the facilities that rubber factories should explore to enhance safety and health. The committee met at 3:00 PM yesterday at the association's headquarters on Pupo Road. Committee members Yang Yongnian, Wu Yunxu, Shi Zhiyun, Li Xin, and others attended. They passed a "Draft Recommendation on Safety and Health Facilities for the Rubber Industry." The contents of the recommendation are excerpted below.

Causes of Fire 124

The recommendation first states the causes of fire and explosion, saying that rubber factories use a large amount of volatile oil as a solvent for rubber, which increases the chances of fire. The main parts that use this solvent are the mixing department, coating department, shoe pasting department, and painting department. The solvent used by rubber factories in this city is gasoline. If it is allowed to evaporate, when the concentration of the evaporated gas in the air reaches a certain limit, it can explode if there are sparks or flames present. Gas explosions require two conditions: (1) the mixture of gas and air must reach a certain ratio, and (2) there must be a suitable heat source with a high temperature to ignite the gas. When these two conditions exist at the same time, an explosion can be triggered. Other potential causes of fire and explosion include electrical equipment, friction between objects, static electricity, boiling varnish, and pressure vessels.

Principles of Fire Prevention 125

The recommendation then discusses the principles of fire prevention, including (1) reducing the evaporation of gasoline, (2) having adequate ventilation in the room to exhaust the evaporated gasoline gas, (3) avoiding the occurrence of sparks, and (4) paying attention to the construction and layout of the factory building so that if a fire occurs in one room, it will not spread to other rooms, and workers must be able to escape to a safe location in a short period of time in the event of a disaster.

A Glimpse of the Recommendations 126

Finally, the recommendations are clarified as follows: (1) Emergency exits: Workshops with fewer than 100 workers must have at least two emergency exits. For every additional 50 workers, one additional emergency exit must be added. (2) Emergency ladders: Workplaces above the first floor must have at least two emergency ladders installed in appropriate locations between every two floors, so that workers can escape to a safe location in a short period of time in the event of a disaster. (3) Fire-fighting equipment: Factories must install fire hydrants and fire hoses in appropriate locations. (4) Fire drills: The factory must select capable workers to organize a fire brigade and conduct regular drills. (5) Workshop layout: Oil boiling rooms, steaming rooms, and steam boiler rooms must be separated from other workshops. (6) Electrical equipment: Special attention must be paid to electrical equipment. (7) Belts: To prevent the danger of static electricity, belts must have grounding devices or be coated with a mixture of graphite and resin on the inside of the belt. (8) For sulfur steaming cylinders, each steaming cylinder must be equipped with a lead safety valve and inspected regularly. (9) Coating rooms: The buildings of coating rooms must be built with fire-resistant materials. (10) Shoe pasting department: The arrangement of female workers' work must not be too crowded. (11) Varnish boiling rooms: Hot varnish rooms must be built with fire-resistant materials. (12) Pulping and scraping machines: Pulping and scraping machines must have grounding devices to prevent the generation of static electricity.

After the Emei Ship Hit a Reef

Telegram Sent Yesterday Afternoon Reported Safety 128

Passengers Delivered to Yichang, Goods Slightly Water-Damaged

Anchored at the Original Location for Initial Repairs Before Determining a Plan

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Chongqing-class river steamer Emei, which departed from Chongqing on the 26th of last month loaded with passengers and goods destined for Yichang, hit a reef in the Fuling area downstream of Chongqing. After efforts to rescue it, it was freed yesterday morning and is undergoing dewatering and repairs. Details are recorded below.

Telegram Reported Safety 129

The Shanghai China Merchants General Bureau received a telegram from the Emei ship yesterday afternoon, informing that the Emei ship, after running aground on a reef, was rescued by a barge sent from Yichang with various rescue equipment. Initially, due to the damage to the bottom of the ship and the intrusion of river water, in order to avoid sinking, the crew actively used machinery to pump water and transferred the passengers to the barge to go to Yichang. They then tried to unload the cargo to reduce the weight and continue the rescue. It was not until yesterday morning that the ship was freed from danger. After the second high tide, it was able to leave the stranded area.

Undergoing Repairs 130

The bottom of the Emei ship has been damaged. First, cement will be used to seal the damaged area. The passengers have been rescued and arrived in Yichang. About half of the cargo has been unloaded, and the bottom of the hold has been water-damaged. After the dewatering is completed, repairs will be carried out to seal the damaged area. The extent of the damage will then be inspected to determine the repair plan. It is said that it will be towed to Shanghai for repairs in a shipyard, as there is no shipyard in the area for repairs.

Yesterday Afternoon, the China Merchants Electric Company

Oil Storage Tank Lost Caution 131

Fortunately, Rescue Was Effective and Did Not Cause a Major Disaster

Mobil Oil Company Has Sent Personnel to Thoroughly Investigate

Two gasoline storage tanks (also known as pumps) installed outside the lines of the workers of the China Merchants Electric Company were placed by the Asia Petroleum and Mobil Oil companies. The gasoline needed by the China Merchants Company is supplied by these two companies, twice a month. Each time, the companies' specially made oil tankers are used for transportation, and then the gasoline is pumped into the storage tanks using belts. At 2:40 yesterday afternoon, Mobil Oil Company delivered the first shipment of gasoline for August, totaling 1,500 gallons, but only half of it (750 gallons) was delivered to the China Merchants Company. When the tanker arrived at the China Merchants Company, the gasoline was pumped into the tank using a belt as usual. Unexpectedly, during the pumping process, the belt suddenly caught fire, and the fire was very fierce. Fortunately, there were many workers at the China Merchants Company. Seeing that the situation was not good, they quickly moved the Mobil Oil tanker away. At the same time, a worker from Mobil Oil Company removed the belt, but the fire was too fierce, and sparks flew into the Asia Petroleum storage tank. Fortunately, there was very little oil in the tank, and no major disaster occurred. Only part of the tank was destroyed, and most of the straw shed between the lines of the workers of the China Merchants Company was burned down. At the same time, fire engines from all districts arrived after hearing the alarm and made every effort to extinguish the fire. The head of the Second District Police Station detained the Mobil Oil Company delivery worker. At about 5:00 PM, Mobil Oil Company sent a Western employee to the China Merchants Company to investigate the truth and released the worker on bail.

After arriving at the restaurant, Yu saw that his friends were gathered there, and after being greeted by the host, he took his seat. At 11:00, the party ended. Yu then ordered the driver to drive to No. 8 Yongji Lane, Wangzhi Road, in the French Concession, to the home of his brother Yu Guanbin. When the car arrived at the entrance of the Yongda Nanhua Store at No. 210 Wangzhi Road, the driver stopped the engine, and Yu got out of the car calmly. Unexpectedly, after walking a few steps,

The Municipal Zoo Opened Yesterday 133

Lions, Tigers, Leopards, Bears, Deer, Foxes, Rabbits, Peacocks, etc., Nothing Was Lacking

The Zoo Site Is Still Too Small, and Land Has Been Purchased to Prepare for Expansion

The Municipal Zoo officially opened yesterday. The opening hours are from 8:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 2:00 PM to 6:30 PM every day. Yesterday, because it was the first time it was opened, the number of visitors was very enthusiastic, and no opening ceremony was held. People were allowed to enter and visit after purchasing tickets. The ticket price was six copper coins for adults and three copper coins for children. A permanent pass costs one yuan per year. The reporter

The Opening of the Municipal Zoo (Photo by Xu Tianzhang) 134

Specially went to observe yesterday, and its various situations are recorded separately below.

A Glimpse of the Zoo 135

The zoo faces the Confucian Temple and was originally the site of a military radio station. The buildings and gardens were dilapidated. After reconstruction, they were completely renovated. The drooping green willows, the sparkling deep pool, the waterside pavilion, the thatched cottage, the rockery, and the winding paths are all like paintings. Although the area is not large, it has its own unique charm. The planners have put a lot of effort into the arrangement. The party and national flags are crossed outside the gate, and the entrance and exit are orderly. The opening rules are posted outside, and there are police officers and zoo staff to maintain order.

Animals in General 136

The animals in the zoo, in addition to the few transferred from the former Public School Garden, are all newly purchased. There are lions, tigers, leopards, bears, deer, foxes, rabbits, wild boars, monkeys, apes, kangaroos, ostriches, peacocks, white cranes, thrushes, and other kinds of mountain birds and domestic animals. They are now placed in various pavilions and sheds. It is said that a large elephant was purchased before and was shipped to Hong Kong, but the elephant suddenly had a foot ailment and was temporarily shipped back. There are also aquatic animals, with five crocodiles being purchased. There is one snake, but because it is not easy to raise and can only live for a maximum of one year, it has not yet been prepared. Currently, there is only one kangaroo among the tropical animals, placed in a house equipped with a hot water heater.

Preparing for Expansion 137

The reporter met with Mr. Shen Xiangrui, the director of the zoo's preparation, and Mr. Lu Hailan, the supervisor of the Mass Education Section of the Education Bureau. According to them, the zoo site is still too small. There is a private vacant lot of about six or seven mu to the west of the zoo, which has been decided to be purchased for expansion. The transaction will be completed soon. The houses behind the zoo, near the Panfang area, were originally the property of the Confucian Temple and will also be recovered in the future, and the houses will be demolished to expand the zoo's site.

Supplementary Ceremony 138

The opening ceremony has not yet been held. The date of the supplementary ceremony has not yet been determined. Because the Municipal Mass Education Center and the Municipal Library have been working for a long time, they have not yet held a ceremony. In the future, a date must be chosen to hold a large-scale ceremony in conjunction with the zoo.

Suddenly, a violent man fired a shot. The bullet hit his back and penetrated his chest, and Yu fell to the ground and died. Seeing that his goal had been achieved, the murderer left. After the police arrived, the murderer had already disappeared. They had to send the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall and wait for the court to examine it this morning. The deceased's brother, Yu Guanbin, and the driver, Ding Jintao, reported to the French police station and asked for the arrest. It is said that the deceased had a six-inch Browning pistol with him, but he did not use it because he did not have time to retaliate.

Yu Feng Yarn Factory Announces Shutdown 139

The board of directors of the Yu Feng Yarn Factory announced that due to the lack of cotton and the significant operating losses over the past six months, the factory will cease operations from 6:00 AM on July 29 of this year. Under these difficult circumstances, in accordance with Article 30 of the Factory Law, which provides for the termination of contracts, the factory is completely terminating the employment contracts of all workers in the factory from today. All previous conditions agreed upon between the factory and the workers and the union are also completely canceled. In accordance with Article 29 of the Factory Law, in addition to paying the workers the wages they are due, the factory will also pay the wages for the advance notice period specified in Article 27 of the same law as follows: (1) Those who have worked continuously in the factory for more than three months but less than one year will be paid an additional ten days' wages. (2) Those who have worked continuously in the factory for more than one year but less than two years will be paid an additional twenty days' wages. (3) Those who have worked continuously in the factory for more than three years will be paid an additional thirty days' wages. In addition, special expenses, such as bathhouse and school subsidies, will be suspended from today. The factory hopes to resume operations as soon as possible within the scope of operational and economic feasibility, but it must be stated in advance that the high cost of expenditure is one of the reasons for the factory's significant losses. Future work plans must be completely reorganized to increase work efficiency and reduce waste. If this is not done, it will not be possible to resume work and achieve the hope of continuing to maintain the factory. The wages and the amount of work will be determined separately when the reorganization is carried out. This is hereby announced.

To all shops in the Concession:

Old Account Books Must Affix Revenue Stamps 144

Otherwise, upon detection, penalties will be imposed according to regulations.

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce issued a notice yesterday to all trade associations, stating: "Regarding the matter of revenue stamps for invoices and account books of shops in the concessions, as per the Ministry of Finance's approval, those that have not been affixed with revenue stamps or have been affixed with an insufficient amount after November 1st of the 18th year should be supplemented to the full amount according to regulations to avoid penalties. This matter is somewhat harsh, and we request your efforts to contend for exemption." After sending a telegram to the Ministry of Finance requesting permission to waive the retroactive surcharge, on the 31st of this month, we received a reply, document number 3060, which stated: "After the implementation of the Revenue Stamp Regulations, any invoices or account books established that do not comply with the affixing of revenue stamps, whenever detected, shall be penalized according to regulations. The Ministry is deeply concerned that merchants may misunderstand the law and not understand the principle of not pursuing past offenses and hopes to be exempt from penalties. A clear explanation has already been given, and all merchants have been ordered to affix them promptly, which is already exceptionally lenient. Now, the request from the Sino-Foreign General Merchandise Trade Association to exempt merchants from affixing revenue stamps to old, discarded invoices and account books that have been set aside before the issuance of the previous approval is even more unreasonable and difficult to approve. It should still be handled in accordance with the previous approval. If they do not quickly affix revenue stamps, they will be executed according to regulations once detected. Do not blame yourselves. You should forward this together to all merchants for compliance, etc." Upon receiving this, we hereby send a notice. We hope you will comply."

Tongyang Steamship Companies Cooperate

Establishing a Joint Business Office 145

Abolishing Price-Cutting Competition

Implementing Public Operation

Jiangbei agricultural products are shipped to Shanghai in large quantities every year. There are two steamship companies in Shanghai, Dada and Datong, which operate ships to various ports in Tongyang. However, in recent years, due to excessive competition, they have been reducing freight rates and secretly giving rebates to each other, which has led to chaotic operations and reduced income. This year, the shipping business on this route has also been relatively quiet. The authorities of the two companies believe that constantly competing by cutting prices is akin to suicide, so they have decided to cooperate in operation, following the example of the six Shanghai-Taiwan companies, to save the shipping industry in a public manner. Yesterday, the two companies established a joint office, and shipping magnates in Shanghai all attended to participate. Details are described as follows:

The Motive for the Union 146

The Tongyang shipping route originally belonged to Dada Company alone, founded by Mr. Zhang Jian of Nantong, and the wharf in Nanshi was also built by Mr. Zhang to develop Jiangbei transportation and transport products to Shanghai. Later, Mr. Lu Bohong also organized the Datong Company to operate on the Tongyang route, and the shipping industry on the Jiangbei route began to compete. Initially, they reduced water freight, and then offered rebates, hoping to increase freight volume, but as a result, the shipping companies' income decreased daily. Four years ago, the two companies proposed cooperation but failed. This year, affected by the commercial downturn, the two companies revived the old proposal and decided to abandon their past mutually-opposed stance and implement cooperation. After discussions between Zhang Xiaoruo, Lu Bohong, etc., they jointly established the Dada Datong Joint Office to develop the shipping industry in a public manner.

Establishment of the Office 147

Dada and Datong Companies joined hands to establish a joint office on the upper floor of the Flour Exchange on Min Guo Road, and each side appointed Zhang Xiaoruo, Lu Bohong, Xu Yihe, Yang Guanbei, Yang Zaitian, Mao Youren, etc. as directors of the board to manage the affairs of the joint office. An audit section was added, with accountant Li Yunliang organizing it. The duties of the joint office are to make freight rates public and unify accounting. The office was formally established at 10:00 AM yesterday, and all directors and important personnel of the two companies attended the opening ceremony.

Report from the Chairman 148

At the opening ceremony, Mr. Du Yuesheng, director of Dada, was publicly elected to deliver a speech. Mr. Du stated that the cooperation between Dada and Datong is to seek the welfare of the people of Tongyang and that everything is done publicly, not monopolistically. Then, Yang Zaitian of Datong reported on the preparations for the cooperation between the two companies and the direction of progress. Chief Auditor Li Yunliang then elaborated on the fact that the joint office was established on the basis of public water freight rates, unified accounting, and improved and expanded operations.

Speeches from Guests 149

The guests who arrived were important figures from the shipping, finance, and yarn mill industries. Liu Hongsheng, general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, took the lead in speaking, detailing the success and benefits of cooperative businesses in England, America, Japan, and Germany. Mr. Liu spoke from his own experience and observations, making it personal and insightful. He said that America's wealth and strength lie in the cooperation of various industries, such as steel, iron, oil, etc. Even small cigarette paper stores in America have a large union of 226,000 stores. In Japan, even small vendors must unite. There are even more cooperative businesses in England and France. Mr. Liu also gave examples. He then said that in China, during the late Qing Dynasty, Mr. Cheng Zhong had the largest business in Shanghai, but it did not last long due to a lack of cooperation. He also said that the Chinese silk mills were the least established and lacked unity, resulting in failure. Finally, he spoke highly about the failure of his own match business due to a lack of unity and the success after uniting. Mr. Liu said that business cooperation can reduce costs and eliminate various expenses, and he hopes that Dada and Datong will progress from cooperation to merger, which will surely lead to faster development. Mr. Qiaolao also gave a speech, praising the various benefits of the union and emphasizing that it is definitely not a monopoly. There were many other speakers, which are not fully recorded.

Forming an Arbitration Committee 150

Within the joint office, an arbitration committee was also formed to resolve disputes between the two companies. The arbitration committee will make public decisions. Li Yunhou, Xi Yushu, Gao Yangzhi, and Lu Xie Rong have been appointed as arbitration committee members. The organization and responsibilities of the committee will be detailed in separate rules.

New Operating Policies 151

Dada and Datong Companies each have four steamships on the Tongyang route. Dada has Daqing, Dayu, Dahe, and Guangxiang, and Datong has Hongda, Longda, Zhida, and Zhengda. After the joint office was established, it was agreed that each company would operate one ship each day. The previous practices of price-cutting and secret rebates will be completely stopped. Freight rates will be set by the committee and publicly followed. There will be no more private price reductions or increased rebates. The cargo manifests of each ship from both companies will be exchanged, and the accounting of the two companies will be calculated and publicly announced by the chief auditor. However, matters such as cabin positions and ticket sales for each ship from both companies will be handled separately and will not involve the joint office.

Group Photo and Dismissal 152

After the meeting, Mr. Du Yuesheng invited important personnel from both companies and all the guests to take a group photo on the sixth floor. Then, refreshments were specially prepared. The meeting adjourned at around 1:00 PM. The operations of the two companies have been jointly managed since yesterday.

Substitute Rickshaw Puller

Gang Intimidates Master for Ten Thousand Gold 153

Diviner Repeatedly Writes Intimidation Letters

Two Criminals Arrested and Sentenced to One and a Half Years of Imprisonment Each

丨 Diviner Sentenced to Four Months of Imprisonment 丨

Gu Pinjian, a native of Jiading, runs the Yongtai Yarn Shop at number 19 Yongkang Lane, Beijing Road. On July 13th of this year, someone suddenly threw an intimidation letter through the window. After Gu unfolded it, the words inside were fierce and sought to extort 10,000 yuan in foreign currency. If he did not agree, his two sons would be in danger in the future, and it would be impossible to redeem them even with tens of thousands of gold. Therefore, he was notified in advance. If he was willing to discuss the payment, he could write the words "Shang Da" (上大) on the door; if not, he could write "Zhong Da" (中大). After receiving the letter, Gu was extremely frightened and reported it to the Laozha Gate Police Station. The head of the police station ordered him to follow the instructions in the letter and write "Shang Da" (上大) on the door.

Indicates Willingness to Negotiate 154

After the criminal gang found　　out, they immediately　　notified Gu Pinjian by telephone,　　limiting him to send the money to the paper waste container next to the urinal in the Weianfang Lane, Haining Road, between 8 and 9 PM on July 16th. Gu reported to the police station again and ordered a large number of Chinese detectives to disguise themselves as workers, wearing old and tattered short clothes, and go to Weianfang to wait. They either lay down or stood, secretly observing the movements. However, the criminal gang was quite alert. Although they had once wandered around the area, they saw people lying on the ground in the lane and suspected they were detectives, so they hesitated and turned back.

Detectives Wait All Night 155

Unable to obtain anything, they also retreated. After Gu reported to the police and detectives were sent, they did not meet again. Later, the criminal gang changed its strategy and threatened Gu by telephone, reaching more than ten times a day, demanding money and gradually reducing the amount from 10,000 yuan to 500 yuan. However, Gu's business has been slow lately, and he could not afford it, so he still ignored them. It was not until the day before yesterday that Chinese detective Shen Dehui and Western detective Heideng of the Huishi Police Station learned of the case.

The police lawyer Wang Yaotang rose and detailed the above situation, saying that the three defendants were being prosecuted under Article 370, Section 3 of the Criminal Law for attempted extortion through intimidation, and requested that they be severely punished. Gu Jinshi, the plaintiff, said that Gu Pinjian is my husband, and after receiving the extortion letter, he was afraid, so he had already

Took Two Children to Guangdong 157

To avoid temporarily. She also　　described the situation,　　saying that the second defendant,　　Wang Maosi, used to be a　　substitute rickshaw puller at my place, so he knew my family situation in detail. The defendant Wang Xuecheng confessed that because Wang Maosi used to work as a servant in Gu's house and knew that Gu was wealthy, he wanted to write a letter to borrow money. He discussed it with me at a certain alley entrance on Xiamen Road. I spent 24 copper coins at Qian Hongsi's divination stall to write a letter. Wang Maosi and I went to the door of Gu's house and threw the letter in from the window, demanding 10,000 yuan in foreign currency. Qian Hongsi confessed that I set up a divination stall at Tangjia Long Xiaocai Lane. Wang Xuecheng came and asked me to write two letters.
