Shaoxing Wine Merchants Telegraph the Tax Affairs Department

Request a Delay in Implementing the Fixed-Quota Tax on Native Wine 164

Shaoxing wine merchants, including Shen Yonghe, collectively telegraphed the Ministry of Finance's Tax Affairs Department yesterday regarding the implementation of the fixed-quota tax on native wine in the seven provinces, which has severely impacted the industry. The telegram stated: "Shaoxing wine is sold throughout the provinces, and its taxes are the highest in the country. Those who bear this huge tax burden are almost all Shaoxing farmers. Shaoxing farmers have historically relied on planting rice and brewing wine for their livelihood. Recently, the rural economy has collapsed, and Shaoxing wine is heavily taxed and slow to sell, often reaching the brink of disaster. The Ministry of Finance is piloting the fixed-quota tax on native wine in the seven provinces, scheduled to be implemented in the winter. A large-scale reform of the tax system and unification of tax revenue should not be interfered with. However, after detailed translation of the regulations, a system of separate collection of production and sales taxes has been established. Tax types in both locations must be balanced. Shanghai is the only sales market for Shaoxing wine, and its sales tax exceeds the production tax by as much as one-third. Suffering this blow, the outlet will inevitably shrink. Moreover, it is well known throughout the country that the older the wine is brewed, the better it is. The shipping deadline is limited to six months, which will eliminate aged wine from the market, resulting in production without sales, and the production quota will inevitably decrease. Saving the national economy and the people's livelihood will have the opposite effect. In particular, affixing tax stamps to a single container often requires as many as three or four stamps, or two or three stamps, forming no distinction and eliminating the perfect old system of one stamp per container. The government only wastes labor and materials, and brewers are most likely to make mistakes, and mistakes will lead to heavy penalties. In addition, all wines that have been affixed with old stamps before this day must be returned and exchanged for new tax stamps on the spot, which is cumbersome and difficult to handle, and is the most excessive harassment. And officials say that it is as easy as lifting a hand, but the law does not apply retroactively. Now, returning old and exchanging new ones requires supplementing some taxes, which is no different from double taxation. These few points are all obstructive and difficult to implement, and the remaining inconsistencies are too numerous to mention. Considering the efforts to alleviate the decline of the rural economy, the whole country is working together to reverse the situation, and Shaoxing farmers are in deep trouble, with only skin and bones left, how can they bear further destruction? We feel deeply pained and cannot remain silent. In addition to submitting a detailed report separately and publicly electing representatives to go to Beijing to petition, we hereby collectively telegraph, begging you to review and quickly suspend the implementation of the new Shaoxing wine regulations, while adopting public opinion, understanding the inconveniences, and allowing separate revisions. We hope to increase tax revenue and care for the people, and allow the regulations to be implemented without obstacles. We anxiously await your orders. Respectfully, Shaoxing Wine Merchants Shen Yonghe, Liu Hexing, Qian Yu, Yue Xing, Yunji, Tang Yuanyuan, Lin Yongyuan, Yu Xiaozhen, Qian Yu Cui, Wang Songmao, Zhang Wanrun, Ye Wanyuan, Zhang Huanji, Zhang Dongming Zhengji, etc."

First Anniversary of the Institute of Forensic Medicine 165

Saving Provincial Funds to Purchase Equipment

Starting to Recruit Forensic Medicine Researchers

The Zhenru Institute of Forensic Medicine has been established for one year, and its internal equipment and detailed planning have been praised by the general public and domestic and foreign experts. August 1st marked the anniversary of the establishment of the institute. The director of the institute, Lin Ji, reported on the facilities established over the past year. The details are recorded as follows:

Holding a Commemorative Ceremony 166

At 8:00 AM yesterday, the institute held a one-week commemorative ceremony. The ceremony was quite grand. All personnel of the institute attended. Director Lin Ji presided over the ceremony. After performing the rituals, Mr. Lin reported on the facilities established since the establishment of the Institute of Forensic Medicine. Then, people from all walks of life expressed their opinions on forensic medicine and encouraged the institute not to interrupt its work. Their words were very pertinent. Finally, the director stood up to deliver a reply. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM after taking a group photo.

Increase Research Equipment 167

Director Lin reported yesterday that the establishment of this institute coincided with the time of national crisis, and the national economy was very depressed. Therefore, the start-up funds for this institute were only more than 20,000 yuan, and the monthly recurring expenses were only more than 4,000 yuan. However, the various facilities and equipment purchases for this institute required funds, which led to extreme difficulties. With the encouragement of colleagues, we tried our best to save expenses, and in one year, we added a mortuary, water table, weighing room, pharmacy, bacteria and serum testing center, animal breeding room, library, printing office, research practice room, etc., and purchased more than 2,000 yuan in equipment and more than 1,500 yuan in medicines, which is how we achieved today's scale.

One Year of Work 168

As for the responsibilities of this institute, they are originally divided into four major tasks: ㈠ identifying and examining cases, ㈡ educating and cultivating forensic medicine talents, ㈢ researching issues related to forensic medicine, ㈣ compiling and translating forms and books related to forensic medicine. In this year, we accepted about 85 difficult cases for identification and examination from various courts, 2,183 ordinary cases, and less than 20 cases from private individuals and groups. As for education, we have now started to recruit 40 researchers, and classes are scheduled to start on September 1. Research work includes the impracticality of using silver needles to detect poison and methods for investigating smoking offenders, etc., and there are many other ongoing research and invention projects. Translation work has not been realized in the past year due to the small number of staff and the intensive work. If the budget can be increased this year, there can also be considerable contributions.

Invite Experts to Cooperate 169

In addition to the technicians at the institute, all technical personnel at this institute also have more than 20 honorary technical commissioners, all of whom are among the best experts in the country. Recently, we have also established close ties with the Natural Science Institute and the Lister Institute, and we plan to cooperate with foreign specialists in China. In short, we are trying our best to find new ways to promote the four major tasks that this institute is responsible for.

The Ciyou Jiaoyang Institute Relocates to a New Site 170

The Shanghai Ciyou Jiaoyang Institute was established by the Chinese Ciyou Association. Its purpose is to take in orphans and widows who are homeless and give them education and training so that they can become independent. In addition, honest and reliable men and women without children are allowed to adopt them to alleviate social problems. Since its establishment, four years have passed in an instant. Hundreds of children have been educated and trained. There are still more than 70 boys and girls in the institute, and the results are quite good. Recently, Ms. Liu Jinfang was hired as the director of the institute. Since taking office, Ms. Liu has been determined to improve the institute's affairs. Because the original site (number 93 Huishan Road) is insufficient, it is heard that it was relocated to number 1052 Tangshan Road, a Western-style house that was formerly the residence of Tan Yankai, the President of the Executive Yuan. The houses there are spacious and the air is fresh, which is very suitable for the children's environment.

The Editor-in-Chief of the Java Chinese Newspaper Arrives in Shanghai 173

The "Java Chinese Newspaper" of Batavia, Dutch East Indies, was founded by local overseas Chinese. Since its publication, it has been popular throughout the South Seas islands. Almost all Dutch residents, including women and children, know the name of this newspaper. Usually, if the local government took any action unfavorable to overseas Chinese, the newspaper would argue based on reason. If any overseas Chinese did not understand the situation in their motherland and misunderstandings arose, the newspaper would do its best to explain. Last spring, during the January 28th Incident, the newspaper made great efforts to encourage overseas Chinese to donate money to save the country. In the past year, according to statistics, the donations remitted to the country through the newspaper's publicity from Java Island alone amounted to no less than one million yuan. It has been found that the greatest achievement of the newspaper is its promotion of overseas Chinese patriotism. The overseas Chinese born in the Dutch East Indies are enthusiastic about their motherland and are regarded as the best in the South Seas Islands. The editor-in-chief of the newspaper, Mr. Guo Keming, is a Java-born Chinese whose ancestral home is in Fujian. He graduated from a Dutch normal school and is proficient in Dutch, German, English, and Malay. Although he has not received education in China, he is extremely protective of his motherland. Everyone says that the new newspaper's achievements could not have been achieved without his perseverance and struggle against the adverse environment. Mr. Guo recently observed that the commercial and industrial situation in Nanyang is declining. He believed that this was an opportunity to encourage overseas Chinese to return to China to invest in and operate industrial enterprises. He specially requested a five-week leave to return to China in person for investigation. He arrived in Shanghai on the Dutch ship "Tsibadak" on the 29th of last month and stayed at the Wai Tan (Bund) Huizhong Hotel. After arriving in Shanghai, he immediately rushed to Nanjing to inspect all the construction of the capital. One morning, he went to Hangzhou for sightseeing. It is heard that he will only stay in Shanghai for a few days and then take the original ship back to Xiamen. Yesterday, Mr. Liu Shimu of the Cultural Department of Jinan University and Mr. Huang Jiping of Shen Bao accompanied him to visit various places. Many other newly arrived overseas Chinese also traveled with them. It is heard that the overseas Chinese community in Shanghai plans to hold a grand welcome party to express their welcome, and hopes that Mr. Guo will stay a few more days to communicate with cultural groups in Shanghai, in order to facilitate the emotional connection between China and Southeast Asia.

Lin Zeruan Released Without Charge 175

Lin Zeruan, a Kuomintang member from Hubei province who has served in party and government agencies in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, was arrested at his residence at No. 87 Chunyang Lane, Dongyouheng Road, on the morning of July 10th by detectives from the Municipal Public Security Bureau and detectives from the Jiaxing Road Patrol Station. According to a report by military police Zhang Zhiyou, he was suspected of plotting to assassinate Finance Minister Song Ziwen, who was going to England to attend the World Economic Conference. He was handed over to the First Special District Local Court. Because the investigation of the Municipal Public Security Bureau was found to be inaccurate, he was sent back to the court. The court ordered that the Patrol Station investigate further and the defendant was released on bail pending further investigation. All of this has been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Xiao Xie Fen of the Special Court held a continued trial. The Patrol Station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that during the adjournment, the inspection department investigated and found that the defendant Lin Zeruan had not committed any crimes in the concession and was indeed a law-abiding citizen. He should be released. After a brief interrogation of the defendant, Judge Xiao ordered Lin Zeruan to be released.

Assassination of Zhang Xinshan

The Three Criminals Have Confessed Unreservedly 176

The reason was fear of being killed, so they struck first.

The debate ended yesterday and a judgment is scheduled.

Zhang Xinshan, a secret agent of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Detective Team No. 62 from Anhui Province, nicknamed "Little Anhui," was stabbed to death by multiple knives at 8:45 AM on the 5th of last month at the entrance of Lane 1, Chongyi Lane, No. 459 Bailaini Mengma Road in the French Concession. He was stabbed 21 times. The Public Security Bureau Detective Team, together with Jin Jiulin, the chief inspector of the special agency of the French Concession Patrol Station, etc., successively arrested the principal criminals Cai Decai, Guo Shanyu, and Guo Yushan from Anhui Province in a straw shed behind Mintini Yin Road and Pudong Guanghua Oil Station, and Pingliang Road. They were first taken away by the Public Security Bureau, interrogated, and then transferred to the French Concession Patrol Station and escorted to the Second Special District Local Court for investigation and detention. At 11:00 AM yesterday, acting Judge Wu Fangqian presided over the trial in the Criminal Court No. 1. The bailiffs brought the defendants to the defendant's column, and Zhang Xinyun, the brother of the deceased, also came to court to await the trial. First, the Patrol Station's lawyer, Yao Zhaodi, described the Patrol Station's investigation, stating that the three defendants were arrested by the Public Security Bureau for the case of the secret agent of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, Zhang Xinshan. The Patrol Station has found that the defendants are indeed the murderers of Zhang. According to the confession of the first defendant, Li Decai, the deceased killed their old man Huang Haiqing (Note: Huang was the detective of the Fourth District of the Jiangsu Water Police Team, stationed in Wusong) at the entrance of Xicheng Lane, Ximen Road on August 6, 1931, under the instigation of Liu Delong, who is still at large. The deceased, now a secret agent of the Public Security Bureau, knew that they were disciples of Huang and would be detrimental to them, so they struck first, colluding with the second and third defendants, Guo Shanyu and Guo Yushan, to wait with Liu at the entrance of Chongyi Lane, Malang Road on the morning of July 5. The two knives and the pistol held by Guo Yushan were all Liu's property. When the deceased passed through the lane entrance, Guo Yushan used his gun to block him, and he and Guo Shanyu stepped forward and stabbed Zhang to death with knives. Liu kept watch on the side. The murder weapon left behind was given to them by Liu. The second and third defendants also confessed to jointly participating in the murder. Now, the Patrol Station is prosecuting the defendants for premeditated murder under Article 284, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law, and requests the court to punish them according to law. He also presented a murder weapon seized by the Patrol Station next to the corpse to the court. Then, Bao Tan (police detective) Cai Jinzhang reported the circumstances of the arrest of the defendants. Zhang Xinyun, the brother of the deceased, also stated the tragic death of the deceased and requested a severe punishment. After the court reviewed the report, it ordered the police to take the defendants down and question them separately one by one. The three defendants all confessed that they were instigated by Liu Delong, who is still at large, to go and commit the murder. The court then appointed lawyer Zhu Taiqing to debate with the Patrol Station's lawyer on behalf of the defendants. After the debate, the court ordered the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the verdict to be announced on August 7. The defendants were still remanded to the Patrol Station to await instructions. The court adjourned after noon.

"Fishing for Aoyu" Sentenced to One Year 181

丨Enticing a Minor Girl to Commit Adultery with Others丨

Cheng Meixian (also known as "Fishing for Aoyu"), who currently hangs a signboard for fortune-telling at the Oriental Hotel on Xizang Road, and the female fortune-teller Ling Qing, Feng Mengyun, the editor of a certain tabloid, etc., were previously sued by Huang Wu, the mother of the late Huang Wenyu, a female disciple of "Fishing for Aoyu," to the First Special District Local Court for harming public morals and harming the family. In the name of fortune-telling, Wenyu was taken to various hotels to prostitute herself. The preliminary trial ruled that the evidence presented by Huang Wu was insufficient and declared the defendants not guilty. However, Huang Wu refused to accept the verdict and filed an appeal with the Second Branch Court. The two courts have completed the trial. Yesterday was the day for the announcement of the verdict. Judge Tian Yuhua opened the court with Judges Zhao and Jiang. All three defendants were not present. Judge Yu announced that the original verdict of Cheng Meixian (also known as "Fishing for Aoyu") being sued for harming public morals was revoked. Cheng Meixian was sentenced to one year in prison for enticing a girl under the age of sixteen to commit adultery with others. Huang Wu's remaining appeals and Cheng Lingqing's appeals were rejected. The accompanying civil suit appeal was rejected.

Kidnapper Zhang Jiancheng Executed by Firing Squad 182

The kidnapper Zhang Jiancheng, also known as Ji Cheng, who was a local, on the afternoon of May 27th of last year, at 5:30 PM, colluded with a gang to carry weapons to the Yifeng Porcelain Factory on Longmen Road and kidnapped Dong Shuying, the director of the factory's purchasing department, and hid him in a bandit's den in Caohejing, demanding a huge ransom. The case was discovered by Lu Liankui, the chief inspector of the General Patrol Station's General Inspection Office, and Feng Zhiming, a detective, who captured Zhang, rescued the hostage, and sent him to the First Special District Local Court. After repeated investigations, it was clarified that Zhang was sentenced to death. The case was submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval and ordered to be executed. Yesterday morning, the Patrol Station escorted Zhang Jiancheng to the Criminal Court No. 3 of the Special Court. The executing judge, Shen Shanzeng, took his seat in the criminal court and ordered the defendant to be brought to court. He briefly questioned his age and籍贯, inquired if he had any last words, and if he had written to his family. However, the defendant was short in stature, and his attitude was calm and without any fear. He said, "I have already sent a letter to my family from prison, and I have nothing else to say." Judge Shen then ordered the defendant Zhang Jiancheng to be sent to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office for execution. Then, the Chinese and Western detectives took Zhang down, together with the entire case file and photos, and escorted him onto the prisoner's car, which drove directly to the execution ground in front of the Second Prison in Caohejing. The prosecutor appointed by the Local Court came to the scene to verify his identity and ordered the police to bind him according to law and execute him by firing squad.

Shop Assistant Stabs Boss After Dismissal 183

Zhang Shixin, the owner of Tongfeng Foreign Goods Store at the Daxin Street entrance of Sima Road in the Public Concession, 41 years old and from Ningbo, was a shrewd and capable manager. One of his shop assistants, named Ah Si, often stayed out at night, violating the store's rules. After Zhang found out, he dismissed him. As a result, Ah Si held a grudge. Unexpectedly, at about 1:30 PM yesterday afternoon, Ah Si suddenly came to the store to argue with Zhang. After a disagreement, Ah Si grabbed the scissors on the counter and stabbed Zhang wildly. Zhang was stabbed a total of nine times in the head, hands, stomach, abdomen, and other places. Seeing that he had caused a major disaster, Ah Si fled. After the stabbing, Zhang was sent to Renji Hospital for treatment by his colleagues. It is said that Zhang's injuries are serious and his life is in danger. The store has reported the case to the Patrol Station for investigation and arrest of the murderer.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks 189

Central Bank Issuance Reserve 168th Inspection Report: This committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible notes by the Central Bank in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations. The 168th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on July 31, 1933. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible notes issued: silver dollars 50,256,879 yuan, including: silver dollar notes 45,698,299 yuan, subsidiary coin notes 4,558,580 yuan. Total amount of convertible note reserve fund: 50,256,879 yuan, including: cash reserve silver dollars 41,054,879 yuan. This cash reserve is deposited in this bank's issuance vault at 36,747,649 yuan, deposited in branches in various ports at 2,500,9329 yuan, and deposited in the same industry at 1,797,901 yuan. Guarantee reserve converted into silver dollars is 9,200,200 yuan. (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued: 417,269.4 yuan. Total amount of customs gold convertible note reserve fund: 417,269.4 yuan. This reserve fund includes 7,004.69 taels of standard gold, which is converted into customs gold 417,269.4 yuan at the fixed price of 5957. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Note Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The inspection results show that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is issued by Chairman Li Fuxun, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Ji of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank on July 31, 1933. The results of the inspection are listed below: The amount of convertible notes issued is 10,936,900 yuan. Weather Report 194

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Shandong coast is cloudy with winds of no fixed direction. The coast here is cloudy with showers and increasing northeasterly winds. The Yangtze River basin has northeasterly to easterly winds of varying strength. The southern East China Sea to the southwest of Kyushu has extremely bad weather with severe cyclones, due to a very large hurricane blowing near Okinawa and then turning northwest. Its center was within 60 miles of the intersection of 25 degrees north latitude and 128 degrees east longitude around 2 PM. The wind force is fierce. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the local temperature was a high of 93.7 and a low of 75.6. On the same day last year, the high was 91.4 and the low was 79.0.

Important News in Education

Pingda High School to Close Next Year 196

Art Institute Closure Comes to an End

(Beiping, 1st) Pingda High School will be closed next year. Funding for the Art Institute was stopped this month, and teachers and staff were not rehired, effectively terminating their positions. Therefore, the closure of the Art Institute has come to an end.

Ping Library Requests Donations of Published Books 197

(Nanjing, 1st) The National Beiping Library has petitioned the Ministry of Education to order all subordinate agencies to donate published books to the library, and sent librarian Hu Ying to Nanjing for discussions. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has ordered all agencies to comply. (Central News Agency, 1st)

Zhejiang Junior High School Graduation Examination Results 198

Grade A: 1157 students, Grade B: 620 students, Grade C: 110 students. All passed and are approved to graduate. 461 students failed and will receive supplementary instruction or repeat a grade. The complete list will be announced and published in the newspaper tomorrow. The regular examination for this year's Zhejiang Province Junior High School graduation examination has concluded, with the results of students who passed all subjects already announced. Students who failed one or two subjects have also undergone supplementary examinations. The supplementary examination papers have now been graded, and the average scores of all subjects in the regular and supplementary examinations have been calculated. A total of 2,421 students participated in the examination. Those approved to graduate include 1,157 students in Grade A, 620 students in Grade B, and 110 students in Grade C. (The top-ranked students in Grade A are from Provincial Fifth Middle School (1st), Provincial First Middle School (2nd), Provincial Second Middle School (3rd), Provincial Fifth Middle School (4th), and Provincial Fifth Middle School (5th).) 172 students must receive supplementary instruction for one semester, 21 students must receive supplementary instruction for one year, 85 students must repeat a semester, and 183 students must repeat a year. 63 students did not attend the supplementary examination, and 10 students did not attend the make-up examination. The complete list will be announced tomorrow outside the Education Department. The ranking by school unit is currently being calculated and evaluated by the Education Department and will be announced soon.

The Ministry of Education Recently Announced Four Types of Curriculum Standards (3)

(4) High School Hygiene 199

First Goal

(1) To enable students to understand modern medical knowledge and the relationship between public health and national health. (2) To cultivate students' ability to solve health problems in life.

Second Time Allocation 200

First academic year, second semester, two hours per week.

Third Teaching Material Outline

(1) The Origins of Modern Medicine: (1) Experiences gained by ancient people regarding diseases. (2) Vesalius and anatomy. (3) The significance of the discovery of blood circulation. (4) The origins of microbiology. (5) Jenner and smallpox vaccination. (6) Medical advancements in the past five years. (2) Characteristics of Modern Scientific Medicine: (1) Scope of application of medical academic knowledge. (2) Comparison between old and new medicine. (3) Treatment methods and medication issues. (3) Social Evolution and National Health: (1) The importance of national health. (2) Leading factors in the development of modern public health. (3) Overview of the implementation of local disease and epidemic eradication in China in recent years. (4) Infant mortality rate and population issues. (5) Social medical organizations. (6) The relationship between education and hygiene. (7) The importance of national eugenics. (8) General principles of genetics. (4) Health and Economics: (1) The relationship between health and economics. (2) Life expectancy issues. (3) Public health and human happiness. (4) Health cooperation system. (5) The understanding and behavior that individuals should have regarding social and national health. (1) Personal hygiene and hygiene regulations. (2) Anatomy and physiology of male and female reproductive organs and their health care (including partner selection and sexual hygiene). (3) The harms of suicide. (4)

Sexual morality. (5) Sexually transmitted diseases and their consequences. (6) The importance of maternal and infant hygiene. (1) Hygiene during pregnancy and childbirth. (2) Early development history of humans and common knowledge of childcare. (7) Family hygiene. (8) Choosing a doctor. (9) Scientific attitude, cooperative spirit, and public morality. Note: The study of this teaching material should be limited to female students.

Fourth Outline of Implementation Methods 201

(1) Homework Requirements:

(1) Classroom lectures and demonstrations using models and charts. (2) Reading of extracurricular reference books. (3) Visits to local doctors and medical institutions. (4) Participation in various public health movements in society.

(2) Teaching Method Key Points:

(1) Teachers should, to the extent possible, make every effort to pay attention to local diseases and local customs in the teaching materials. (2) Teachers should supplement or delete certain teaching materials according to the gender of the students. (For example, female students should study more about family hygiene and personal health care, while male students should study more about social issues.) (3) The teaching materials on sexual hygiene in item (5) should be taught in separate classes for male and female students. The teachers hired should, in principle, be of the same gender as the students. (4) Classroom teaching should ideally start with discussions of practical life problems. (5) Teachers should provide students with opportunities to ask questions. (6) Teachers should be responsible for guiding students on the elements of a healthy life. (7) Health examinations should be conducted once every academic year. If physical defects or deformities are found, efforts should be made to correct them. (8) In addition to hiring school police, schools should, to the extent possible, organize a Health Education Committee to oversee the design and administrative matters of health education within the school. (9) Schools should, to the extent possible, fully equip themselves with sanitation facilities and strive to make the environment fully healthy in order to promote the realization of students' healthy living and environmental integration. (End)

Flexible Measures for High School Entrance Examination Repeaters 203

Those Who Fail One Subject Besides Chinese, English, Math, Physics, and Chemistry

May Be Issued Certificates for Advance Enrollment as Probationary Students

The Shanghai Education Bureau yesterday instructed private colleges and universities and private middle schools at all levels in the city participating in this year's high school graduation examination, stating: "Regarding the Ministry of Education's Instruction No. 7394, Jiangsu Provincial Education Department, Fujian Provincial Education Department, and Nanjing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau have successively reported that they request temporary approval to issue certificates to students who failed the middle school graduation examination repeater courses so that they can apply for colleges and universities. The Ministry has reviewed the situation and found that the middle school graduation examinations in various provinces and cities are being conducted earnestly, so there are still a considerable number of students who failed the repeater courses. In order to assist the majority of young people so that they can continue their education, special flexible measures will be taken this year. For all students in the high school graduation examination, if they fail one subject after retaking the course, other than the five subjects of Chinese, English, Mathematics, Physics, and Chemistry, the Bureau will issue a certificate to allow them to apply for colleges and universities first. After being admitted, they will be treated as probationary students. After passing the examination in each failed subject in the next high school graduation examination, a high school diploma will be issued. After verification by the colleges and universities where they are studying, they will be treated as regular students. Students who fail the junior high school graduation examination and apply for higher education with equivalent qualifications are free to do so without the need for a separate certificate. In addition to separate orders, this order is hereby issued for your information and for you to instruct your subordinates accordingly." Therefore, in addition to printing certificates for application and issuance, this order is hereby issued for your information.

University Joint National Salvation Propaganda Team Works Hard 204

Hunan and Zhejiang Teams Have Already Departed

Anhui Team Returned to Shanghai Yesterday to Report on Work

The Shanghai University Student Union organized a national salvation propaganda team during the summer vacation, which went to various places to work very hard. All teams in Jiangxi, Hunan, Zhejiang, and Jiangsu have successively departed and arrived in various places to conduct oral and written propaganda, which is quite popular among the people. It is reported that the work of the Third Team (Anhui Team) has been completed. The team leader, Yang De'an, led all team members back to Shanghai by ship. After landing, each team member went to the general headquarters of the University Union Propaganda Team to report on the work in Anhui in great detail. According to the team leader, Yang De'an, who spoke to a Shanghai News reporter, the propaganda team, after arriving in Anhui, immediately divided into urban and rural groups for the convenience of work, and appointed Zhang Hao and Hong Xiao Chen as the leaders of each group. Then, they led the team to work in various places. The rural group paid special attention to propaganda in rural areas, so they gained the sympathy of the general farmers. The urban group gave popular lectures in busy towns more than ten times, with a total audience of no less than 50,000 to 60,000 people. They are currently compiling a detailed work report.

Reaction to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund Not Recruiting Agricultural Students 206

Mu Ouchu and Others Wrote to Question

Request Adding Two Agricultural Students

The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund's board of directors has decided to select 20 students to study in the UK, which has attracted the attention of the academic community. However, upon investigation, all subjects in natural and social sciences are available, but the agricultural subject, which is deeply related to China, is missing. Agricultural leaders Mu Ouchu, Shao Bingwen, Cai Wuji, and twenty to thirty others have specifically raised objections to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee on this matter. The original manuscript is excerpted below.

Letter from Mu Ouchu et al. 207

Respectfully, we recently read in the newspaper that your committee's 17th board meeting decided to send 20 students to study in the UK with Boxer Indemnity funds. The subjects of study include English literature, Western history, law, politics, mathematics, geography, geodesy, medicine, public health, civil engineering, and other disciplines, but agricultural science is missing. Recently, the social clamor for rural revitalization has been rampant, and the government has specific organizations to promote it, which is more important than any other discipline. If agricultural science is missing, it seems inappropriate from a pragmatic point of view. Moreover, China's rural revitalization is extremely tense, and there is a shortage of talent. The British agricultural experiment stations are advanced in all countries. Sending students to study agriculture in the UK with Sino-British Boxer Indemnity funds will have a greater effect than other disciplines. We respectfully ask your committee to include two agricultural students in the plan. This matter concerns the national public interest, so we dare not remain silent. We hope you will investigate and implement it. To the best of our friendship, we address the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee, etc.

Reply from the Boxer Indemnity Fund Committee 208

Direct reply: We have received your letter requesting that two agricultural students be added to this committee's case of sending students to study in the UK. Mr. [Mu Ouchu]'s concern for academics and promotion of agriculture is admirable. Regarding the allocation of subjects for this committee's selection of students, it has been determined. Not having agricultural science is indeed a subject that our country currently needs. This committee has discussed this when allocating subjects. The United Kingdom is an industrial nation, so it was unanimously decided to postpone the selection of students for the agricultural subject. We will certainly report this to the next board meeting and refer to Mr. [Mu Ouchu]'s letter in the next selection of students next year. Thank you for your intention. We hereby reply and hope you will inform your colleagues listed. We apologize for not replying to each of them individually. Best regards to Mr. Mu Xiangyue, Management Office of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund.

Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union

Dispute Arises in Workers' Children's Free School 210

British American Tobacco Factory in Pudong Undermines Labor Education

The workers' children's free school established by the Shanghai Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union previously signed an agreement with the factory on April 1, 1929, stating that the factory would subsidize the union 750 yuan per month as operating expenses and stipulating that the factory had the right to send representatives to inspect the teaching. Over the years, everything has been fine. Unexpectedly, on June 23, the factory suddenly sent a letter to the union, claiming that the school was not well-managed and requesting termination of the contract. The union immediately submitted a report to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau to negotiate on reasonable grounds. During the mediation at the Social Affairs Bureau, the factory proposed the following conditions: (1) The school board must consist of five representatives from the capital, five representatives from the labor, and five representatives from the Municipal Party Department, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Education Bureau. (2) The monthly subsidy must be collected directly from the factory by the principal. The union stated that it did not object to the factory's proposed improvements, but the factory should not interfere with its sovereignty. The Education Bureau and the party and government organs should be in a supervisory position, and the union should handle the appointment of school board members, with the factory having no right to interfere. As a result, the mediation was unsuccessful. Yesterday morning, the union sent all members of the board of directors and supervisors to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau to petition. The Municipal Party Department sent Zhang Sheng and the Social Affairs Bureau sent Wang Xian Qing to receive them. The union representatives presented a petition and denounced the factory's attempt to undermine the treaty under the guise of improvement, which was a major issue concerning the education of 8,000 workers' children. They requested that the original contract be maintained. The result was very satisfactory. The union, because the factory violated the terms and undermined labor education, had already scheduled an emergency representative meeting to discuss countermeasures. It was also heard that the school board held an emergency meeting last night, as the start of the school year was approaching. It was decided to maintain the school independently and appoint Shen Yu as the principal. Classes are scheduled to begin on the 28th of this month. Today, a notice has been issued to start enrolling new students.

Minzhi Junior High School Adds Scholarship Quotas 211

Minzhi Junior High School on Avenue Road had outstanding results in this year's graduation examination, so there was a large number of students from outside the school applying for admission and students from the affiliated elementary school were also keen to enroll. The first grade Class A is now full, so 50 new students will be added to the first grade Class B. In order to provide preferential treatment to poor students, ten scholarship quotas have been set up, half for boys and half for girls, with tuition waived. Graduates of the city's graduation examination with excellent academics and conduct may be recommended by their original school to take the exam on August 20.

Huiling Middle School Expands Commerce Department 212

Huiling Middle School in Xinlonghua, West Shanghai, has been established for more than ten years. The school has always been strict in its training and teaching. In this year's examination, 100% of the junior high school students and 91% of the senior high school students were approved to graduate. It is heard that the school, in view of the current social trend of emphasizing vocational education, has decided to expand the original commerce department, add courses, and is looking for suitable teachers. The new teachers who have been hired for the next semester include Gu Yongquan, Hu Yipeng, and Zhang Kan. The school is scheduled to hold an entrance examination on August 21. A large number of people have been enthusiastically registering in recent days.

East Asia Boy Scout Training Class

Holds Lushan Summer Camp 213

Depart Today on the Jiangjing Steamer to Jiangxi to Practice Various Outdoor Activities

The East Asia Physical Education College in Lujiawan, Shanghai, recognizing the lack of Boy Scout instructors in China, established a Boy Scout Instructor Training Class, invited domestic Boy Scout experts to serve as professors, and has achieved considerable success since its establishment. This year's summer training class has a very large number of students. The training methods are divided into three types: indoor, outdoor, and teaching practice. It is heard that the indoor theory courses have been intensively trained within three weeks, without regard to the day of the week, and have been completed. Therefore, it has been decided that the national regiment leader Qu Yue, coaches Sun Yixin, Gong Jingyuan, and Jin Shaowen will lead the students on the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangjing Steamer to Lushan, Jiangxi, today for a summer camp to practice outdoor life. There will also be a 24-hour travel and reconnaissance, tracking, map-making, surveying, campfire, field warfare, and various course competitions. The camp will be dismantled on the 13th and returned to Shanghai for a graduation examination. The Boy Scout General Association will send personnel to invigilate the examination. Diplomas will also be issued by the central government. All students are energetic and studying hard. It is expected that the results will be very good.

Hong Kong-Shanghai Table Tennis Competition Preparations Busy

無錫晋陖隊亦派將來滬會師

Wuxi Jinling Team Also Sending Players to Shanghai

自香港乒乓冠軍隊東方體育會來滬之消息傳出後、滬上乒乓團體、又　活躍現象、茲悉乒乓聯合會日來正忙於籌備、男子宿舍問題及比賽球室、已由該會徐多向中華儉德會接洽就緖、

Since the news of the Hong Kong Table Tennis Champion Team, the Eastern Athletic Association, coming to Shanghai, Shanghai's table tennis groups have become active again. It is known that the Table Tennis Association has been busy preparing in recent days. The problem of male dormitories and competition rooms has been settled by Xu Duo of the Association contacting the China Jian De Association.

截至昨日止、接到參戰通知書者已有廣東·郵甲·也是·市甲·古氏等隊、而同時向該會要求一親港隊風味者、有精一·中皂·中信·曦光·强靑甲·江稜·愛樂等隊、卽遠在無錫之晋陵隊、亦致函該會徐多、準備日内遣將與港隊會師滬上、惟港隊留滬日期有限、故除晋陵隊外、其餘未擬定各隊、尙須分别審核

The Administrative Inspectorate of the Fifth District of Jiangsu Province is actively preparing for the sports meet in this district (Shangnan and Chuansha counties), as the deadline set by the provincial department of August 25th is approaching. It held its first preparatory committee meeting at the agency yesterday. Committee members Cao Zhenfei, He Jiyun, Shen Jing, Qian Pansheng, Xiong Zhugao, Cao Weizhou, Xue Songgan, Shi She, Zhu Wanqu, and Jin Zuobin attended. 春秋酸葡萄哲學  林濚

The Sour Grapes Philosophy of the Spring and Autumn Period Lin Ying

從前有一隻還算聰明的狐狸，這一天，看見一架熟透了的葡萄，得垂涏三尺；可惜架子太高，百計不能到手；向着葡萄望了半天，只得無精打彩的走了開去，自已欲安慰着自已道：「那葡萄一定還酸得很呢！」

Once upon a time, there was a fairly clever fox. One day, it saw a vine of ripe grapes, making its mouth water. Unfortunately, the vine was too high, and it tried every possible way but could not reach them. After staring at the grapes for a long time, it had to walk away listlessly, comforting itself, saying, "Those grapes must still be very sour!"

這叚新聞流傳到人間，有些人便學會了一種聊以自慰或解嘲的方法。例如某甲單戀久久，毫無結果，只得罷手；罷手自然不甘，便會竭力從那夢寐不忘的女人身上導出某些缺點。又如舉子落第，便假設榜上題名也許會發生某種不幸；財迷望見黄金而無以得之，便也會照幾聲銅臭。

When this story spread among people, some learned a way to comfort or make fun of themselves. For example, if someone, let's call him A, had a long unrequited love with no results and had to give up, naturally he would be unwilling to do so, and would try his best to find some flaws in the woman he could not forget. Or, if a scholar failed in the imperial examination, he would assume that some misfortune might occur if his name were on the list; if a money-grubber saw gold but could not obtain it, he would also imagine the smell of copper coins.

這種方法，久而久之，便形成了一種頗有權威的生活哲學，或處世哲學。這哲學可以名爲自解哲學；如果要追溯到那來歷，便可以呌做「酸葡萄哲學」這名字就活潑得多了。

Over time, this method has formed a rather authoritative philosophy of life, or a philosophy of dealing with the world. This philosophy can be called the "philosophy of self-explanation"; if we want to trace its origin, we can call it the "sour grapes philosophy," which is a much more vivid name.

今日之酸葡萄哲學，好像在古老的中國特别發達。原來悠遠的封建社會之聖賢一向便以「忍」敎人，而造成了中國人之普遍的善於自安。到了今日，例如東四省淪亡之後，許多人還要搖頭搖尾道：「這正是中國人的好敎訓呢！」講這話的人自然不主張快快抗爭，而主張十年生聚之類，另外一些人聽了此話也便不暇思索的做那十年生聚之類的偉業去了。酸葡萄哲學發展到這般地步可謂猗歟盛哉。

Today's sour grapes philosophy seems to be particularly developed in ancient China. Originally, the sages of the distant feudal society always taught people to "endure," which created the Chinese people's general ability to be content. Today, for example, after the loss of the four northeastern provinces, many people still shake their heads and wag their tails, saying, "This is a good lesson for the Chinese people!" People who say this naturally do not advocate quick resistance, but advocate things like ten years of regeneration. Others who hear this do not bother to think and go do great things like ten years of regeneration. The development of sour grapes philosophy to this point can be called magnificent.

這般說來，酸葡萄哲學是弱者自慰哲學，是貪求者的解嘲哲學，同時是狡者的愚民哲學；統而名之，則爲自欺欺人哲學。

In this way, the sour grapes philosophy is the philosophy of self-consolation for the weak, the philosophy of self-deprecation for the greedy, and at the same time, the philosophy of fooling the people for the cunning; collectively, it is the philosophy of deceiving oneself and others.

說到弱者之以酸葡萄哲學聊以自慰，絶不能如唯心論者般解釋爲心理缺陷，而正是社會有以造成之。因爲社會太不平等，所以許多人處處受壓迫，不能有正當的自我發展，而終於只得拿酸葡萄哲學自解了，這裏，這葡萄而且舊了。可是我們相信世界終究會好。的那時無論是自欺或欺人的哲學都會消滅。

When it comes to the weak using the sour grapes philosophy to console themselves, it must not be explained as a psychological defect as idealists do, but rather as something caused by society. Because society is too unequal, many people are oppressed everywhere and cannot have proper self-development, and finally have to use the sour grapes philosophy to explain themselves. Here, these grapes are also old. But we believe that the world will eventually be better. At that time, whether it is self-deception or deceptive philosophy, it will disappear.

炎夏散記  黄影呆

Random Notes in the Scorching Summer Huang Yingdai

「啊呀」？…冰啊！…冰要喂冰啊……賣冰的孩子們，在烈日之下，馬路之中，高喊着同樣的賣冰聲，他們走過的時候，總是在來不及的奔跑怕的是冰要溶化啊！

"Ah!"... Ice! ... Ice, ice for sale..." The children selling ice, under the scorching sun, in the middle of the road, shouted the same cry of selling ice. When they walked by, they were always running as fast as they could, afraid that the ice would melt!

在那邊的角子上，一個賣報的老頭子，冬天，太陽整日的曬在他身上，如果不是雨雪天呢，不穿皮裘，也正和高樓中的圍爐者同様的温暖，可是這幾天，糟糕，火一般的太陽曬得他頭上幾乎要出火了。

Over there in the corner, an old man selling newspapers. In the winter, the sun shines on him all day long. If it weren't for the rainy and snowy days, he wouldn't wear a fur coat and would be as warm as those who huddle around the stove in tall buildings. But these days, it's terrible. The fiery sun is shining so hard that his head is almost on fire.

鴿龍式的屋子裏，風一些也吹不着太陽老是逼着你，裏面眞不能住人了，走吧，到那裏去？還是隔壁的弄堂裏，曬不着太陽，吹得着輕風，坐在矮凳上談天說地，誰說不是莫于山第二？

In the pigeon coop-like house, the wind can't reach you at all, and the sun is always forcing you. It's really impossible to live inside. Let's go, where to go? Or in the alley next door, where the sun doesn't shine and a light breeze blows. Sitting on a low stool, chatting about everything under the sun, who says it's not the second Mount Mogan?

在中午的時節，雖是在熱閙的南京路上，行人也稀少了許多。摩登女士，時裝少年，不知匿跡在何處，怕是太陽要曬黑皮膚吧，不到夜晚是不肯輕易的出來吧！

At noon, even on the bustling Nanjing Road, there are far fewer pedestrians. Modern ladies and fashionable young men, I don't know where they are hiding. They're probably afraid that the sun will darken their skin. They won't come out easily until night!

前天因爲有些事情出去，喊了一輛黄包車回來，車夫在烈日中狂奔，已是奔得滿頭大汗，他對我說，夏天拉車，上面有太陽的逼曬，下面有柏油　脚底，再苦是没有，我聽見了非常的不忍，到寓下車，多給了幾個銅子他，也算是表示我的同情啊！

The day before yesterday, because I had something to do, I hailed a rickshaw to come back. The rickshaw puller ran wildly in the scorching sun, already running with sweat all over his head. He said to me, pulling a rickshaw in the summer, the sun is shining on you from above, and the asphalt is scorching your feet from below, there's no suffering greater than this. I felt very sorry when I heard this. When I got off at my residence, I gave him a few extra coppers, which was also a way to show my sympathy!

隔弄小樓的一角，望去有幾個妙齡的少女，整個的午後，坐在電風傘下，聽的，有無綫電，留音機：吃的，是西瓜，冰汽水，伊們的生活是多麽舒服，眞羨煞了窮措大呢，造物爲什麽是如此的不平等啊！

Looking out from the corner of a small building in the alley, there are several young girls. All afternoon, they sit under the electric fan, listening to the radio and phonograph; eating watermelon and ice soda. Their lives are so comfortable. It really makes poor scholars envious. Why is creation so unequal!

散絃  葉奕願

Loose Strings Ye Yiyuan

學校的門口，有雨爿商店，可以保發大財的：一是洗衣作，再一是食物館。

At the school gate, there are two types of stores that are guaranteed to make a fortune: one is a laundry, and the other is a food shop.

學校裏休息十分鐘的時間内，有兩處地方是最擁擠的：一是小便處，一是消費合作社。

During the ten-minute break at school, there are two places that are the most crowded: one is the urinal, and the other is the consumer cooperative.

有許多學生，在平時雖不用功；然而在大便時，總得要拿本小說來解解閒。此之可謂中國新靑年的特有的一點藝術。

Many students, although they don't study hard at ordinary times, always have to bring a novel to relieve boredom when they defecate. This can be said to be a unique art of Chinese new youth.

鄉下姑娘，到大都市裏來讀了半年的書，回去時，在伊的衣食住行方面，一定可以故試得出，伊是曾經趕過了一次大革命！

A girl from the countryside, after studying in a big city for half a year, when she returns, you can definitely tell from her clothing, food, housing, and transportation that she has experienced a great revolution!

讀書是要靜的。從前有一個先生對我說：「你讀書不要發出聲來，因爲發出聲來，就等於出了氣。老酒出了氣，等於屁；讀書而出了氣，也是得不到益處的啊」！

Reading requires quiet. Once, a teacher said to me: "Don't make noise when you read, because making noise is like letting out air. Old wine that has let out air is like a fart; reading and letting out air will not get you any benefits!"

東北四連長  張恨水

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast Zhang Henshui

第十二回　寒賤苦從戎病夫落伍　犧牲甘解甲戰士多情

Chapter Twelve: The Poor and Humble Suffer in the Military, the Sick and Weak Lag Behind; Sacrificing Themselves Gladly to Disarm, Soldiers are Sentimental

盛世民又說，在軍營裏當軍官，至少當了營長以上的官，上了陣線，不會安全些。若說連排長，那是和弟兄們一様的受罪。排長是不必說，打起仗來，他带着一排人，先上前。連長也是緊緊的跟着三排人。打起仗來，有正正的全旅全團不回來的，連長那兒安全得了？

Sheng Shimin also said that being an officer in the military camp, at least a battalion commander or higher, would not be safer on the front lines. As for company and platoon leaders, they suffer the same as the brothers. Platoon leaders don't need to be said, when fighting, they lead a platoon of people to go forward first. The company commander also closely follows the three platoons. When fighting, there are entire brigades and regiments that don't come back, how can the company commander be safe?

江氏道：不打仗，没有功勞，那裏升得了官？盛世民道：勸人去當兵的，總是說可以升官發財。其實幾萬人裏頭，才挑出一個師旅長來，除了自已要有那能耐外，還要命運高，上個十次二十次火線，才有升大官的希望。别說上了火線，那槍砲子彈打得天上是火，地下是煙，在火線上有個三天四天的話，耳朶都會震聾。兩三天不吃飯，兩三天不喝水，那是極平常的事。我也想破了，不幹也罷。我們八塊錢餉，折成六塊四毛錢，還要四五十天發一回，扣了火食，能買雙襪子，捎一封家信，就算不錯。所以當大兵的人，七八年不回去，那是常事。你呌他拿什麽臉子回去？

Jiang said: If you don't fight, you don't have merit, how can you get promoted? Sheng Shimin said: Those who persuade people to join the army always say that they can get promoted and make a fortune. In reality, only one division or brigade commander is selected from tens of thousands of people. In addition to having the ability, you also need to have good fortune. You need to go to the front lines ten or twenty times to have hope of getting a high rank. Not to mention going to the front lines, the guns and bullets are fired so hard that the sky is fire and the ground is smoke. If you are on the front lines for three or four days, your ears will be deafened. It is very common to not eat for two or three days, and not to drink water for two or three days. I've thought it through, I might as well not do it. Our eight yuan salary is discounted to six yuan and forty cents, and it is paid every forty or fifty days. After deducting food expenses, it's good enough to buy a pair of socks and send a letter home. So it is common for soldiers not to go back for seven or eight years. How can you ask him to go back with any face?

這些話說得江氏默然無言。這天晚上，江氏一人睡在坑上，仔細想了一想，聽說連長是六十塊錢薪水，二十塊錢辦公費。若是打個八折，只好六十四塊錢，又要拿錢出來辦公，又要扣火食，還是四五十天一回，一個月也就不過三十來塊錢罷了。自已的姑娘，無論是說性格兒，模様兒，和他的能耐，那一様不是百裏挑一挑出來的。憑着這様的人不難道要挑一個掙二三十塊錢的姑爺，還找不出來嗎？你看，趕上定親，兩家都答應了，這是多要緊的時候。可是這位趙連長，倒在這個日子，遇上了總司令檢閱軍隊，抽不開身來。（一四六）

These words made Jiang silent. That night, Jiang slept on the kang alone, thinking carefully, and heard that the company commander's salary was sixty yuan, and twenty yuan for office expenses. If it is discounted by 20%, it would only be sixty-four yuan. He also has to take money out for office work, and deduct food expenses, and it is still every forty or fifty days, so it is only about thirty yuan a month. My daughter, whether it's her character, her looks, or her ability, isn't everything one in a hundred? With such a person, is it not difficult to find a son-in-law who earns twenty or thirty yuan? Look, it's time to get engaged, and both families have agreed. This is a very important time. But this Company Commander Zhao happened to meet the commander-in-chief inspecting the troops on this day and couldn't get away. (146)

普陀的梵音洞  衛術

The Sound of Brahma Cave in Putuo Wei Shu

乘着　曲折的後山之山腰，足邊茸茸地長着野草之叢，來到梵音洞，是午前十一時。

Arriving at the Sound of Brahma Cave at 11 AM, riding along the winding mountainside of the back mountain, with clusters of weeds growing lushly at the edge of the foot.

梵音洞之出名，奇妙傳說比之崢嶸的山色，是更其重要的，在那裏，有着會告訴人來生變作什麽的地方。

The fame of the Sound of Brahma Cave, the wonderful legends, is more important than the towering mountain scenery. In there, is a place that can tell people what they will become in their next life.

洞在山麓洞底蓋有一座廟，進得山門，要越過百十砐下行的石級。途中樹一禁止捨身投淵的木牌，立在那裏望峻峻的山巖下面，確乎是　惴然的。旣讓人曉得來生，又勸人不可妄求，又是什麽意思呢。

There is a temple at the foot of the mountain at the bottom of the cave. To enter the mountain gate, you have to cross a hundred or so steps of downward stone steps. Along the way, there is a wooden sign prohibiting people from giving up their bodies and throwing themselves into the abyss. Standing there and looking down at the steep cliffs below is indeed frightening. What is the meaning of both letting people know their next life and advising them not to seek it rashly?

越往下走，心就越是陰沉沉的，滿身一個洞，也像别的洞那麽凉快，黝暗，並没有什麽不相似的地方。

The further down you go, the more gloomy your heart becomes. The whole body is in a cave, as cool and dark as other caves, and there is nothing dissimilar about it

Anniversary of the Completion of the General Headquarters Building 215

Yesterday marked the first anniversary of the completion of the Chinese Academic and Arts Society's general headquarters building on Avenue Albert. The Society's members in Shanghai held a dinner party at 8 p.m. to celebrate. More than 40 people from academic circles attended, including Ou Yuanhuai, Ma Zongrong, Zhang Zhongdao, Zhou Xianwen, Lu Guixiang, Li Zongwu, Luo Zongluo, Zhu Shaoqing, Qian Gecuan, and Zhang Menglin. Lively discussions took place during the meal, and the party ended happily at 9 p.m.

Railway Ministry Dispatches Personnel

To Take Over the Two Roads Shanghai Rotary School 216

The Shanghai Rotary School at the North Station was established by the Two Roads Administration Office ten years ago. Now, in order to comprehensively improve the education of employees' children, the Railway Ministry has decided to take over the school. At 9 a.m. on July 31, the Railway Ministry dispatched Zhang Weigao, a staff member of the Yucai Section of the General Affairs Department, leading the new principal He Xiru (who was not present) represented by Sun Biwu, to the Administration Office to take over. The Administration Office sent Director Wang of the Personnel Section of the General Affairs Department to jointly hand over the school. The Standing Committee member Zheng Jian of the Two Roads Special Party Department attended to provide guidance. The former principal, Li Jingwei, handed over the school equipment, documents, and other items, which were received by Sun, the representative of the new principal. It is reported that the existing teachers, if qualified, will be retained and will continue to work from August 1.

Sports

Rotary Cup Shanghai International Tennis Chinese Players Determined 217

Zheng Zhaojia, Yu Tianguang, Wang Wenzheng, Ma Anquan

International Tennis Today Convened Representatives from Various Countries

-Chinese Tennis Committee Decides Open Singles Finals on the 9th-

The Rotary Cup Shanghai International Tennis Tournament, a competition among five nations, today was convened by the Xie Jin Association to gather representatives from various countries at the Metrojole Hotel on Jiangxi Road for a meeting to draw up the competition order and discuss all related matters. It is said that the United Kingdom will not participate this year.

The Chinese Tennis Committee met yesterday afternoon at Dun Tuomo, attended by Hu Xiansheng (Chairman), Hu Yunlai, Li Baojun (represented by Zhou Jiajun), Ling Xitao, and Zhou Jiaqi. Resolutions were as follows:

(1) Selected Zheng Zhaojia, Yu Tianguang, Wang Wenzheng, and Ma Anquan as representatives of the Chinese team to participate in the Rotary Cup and Robber Cup.

(2) Appointed Li Baojun as manager of the Chinese team and representative of the Chinese team to attend the Rotary Cup representatives' meeting of various countries.

(3) Set August 9 (Wednesday) as the final date for the open singles competition. All rescheduled quarter-finals should be arranged by the players themselves and completed before the 9th, without further rescheduling.

National Games

Yesterday Receiving the Venue 218

Preparatory Committee Holds Regular Meeting

(Nanjing, 1st dispatch) The National Games Preparatory Committee resolved in a regular meeting tonight: (1)

The office location of the committee, regarding the general affairs, some staff will first move to the Central Stadium to work. (2) Reviewed and approved the work plans of the five groups: transportation, hygiene, publicity, security, and national martial arts. (3) Reviewed and approved various competition rules and handed them over to the general affairs group for printing. (4) Scheduled to hold another meeting next week at 8 p.m. The National Games Preparatory Committee dispatched Lei Zhen, Peng Baichuan, and Zhang Xinfu on the 1st to officially receive the venue. Starting from the 2nd, they will check the prizes and stationery. Regarding the water problem, Xia Guangyu and Zhang Xinfu and two other individuals have been assigned to measure the venue and visit the old pond, and the water from the artesian well will be poured into the pond for drinking. The previous proposal to install tap water may be abandoned due to funding constraints.

Mr. Liu Shenzhan

Suggests Postponing the National Games 219

To Save Economical resources and Time

Should Be Postponed to Mid-April Next Year

Also Serves as the National Preliminary Round for the Far Eastern Games

Mr. Liu Shenzhan issued an express telegraph yesterday, suggesting that this year's Tenth National Games be postponed to April next year. The reason is that since the Games and Conference were held this year, and the Far Eastern Games will be held in the Philippines in mid-June next year, China will inevitably hold another preliminary round. To save huge expenses and the precious time of young people, it is indeed necessary to postpone the Games to be combined with next year's national preliminary round, he said. His words are reasonable, and the original text is excerpted as follows:

The Tenth Far Eastern Games are scheduled to be held in Manila, Philippines, from June 9th to 17th next year (1934), and the Philippines has telegraphed to China and Japan to participate. Therefore, in April or May next year, China must hold a preliminary round to participate in the Far Eastern Games and select athletes, without any doubt. Since a preliminary round must be held in April or May next year, and another meeting will be held in October this year, holding meetings is never too much, but how can we not consider the national economy and the precious time of athletes? Moreover, the National Sports Conference last year resolved that the National Games should be held once every two years and be connected with international sports events. This is what promoters of sports should pay attention to. China's transportation is inconvenient, and its economy is declining. Holding a National Games is not an easy task, especially compared to Europe and the United States holding the World Games. According to estimates, each time a National Games is held, the expenses of the central government and various provinces and cities will be no less than several millions of yuan. Holding National Games every year and building a magnificent central sports field at Linggu Temple, which is far from the city, are equally uneconomical. To save national funds and the precious time of young people, this year's meeting should be postponed to April or May next year, which can achieve multiple benefits.
